atha śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe pañcamī umā saṃhitā prārabhyate śrī gaṇeśāya namaḥ śrī gaurī śaṅkarābhyām namaḥ atha pañcam umā saṃhitā prārabhyate yaḥ gante su vananī tam sāṃvitū guṇa vartī māyām atītya sthitaḥ satya ānandam ananta bodham ayalam brahma ādi śaṃjñā alpa dam nityam sarva samanvaya ādika gatām pūrṇam śivam bhīmahi ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ sūta sūta mahā prājña vyāsa śiṣya namaḥ astu te caturthī koṭi krudh akṣyā śrāditā saṃhitā tvayā atha umā saṃhitā antam svan āryāna saminvitaṣu śṛhi śaṃbhoḥ caritram sāmbhasya paramātmanaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca śṛṇuta śubham śāṅkaram caritam divyam mukti mukti pradam param iti īdṛśam puṇya praśnam pṛṣṭavān muni sat tamaḥ vyāsaḥ sanat kumāram vai śaivam saṃcaritam jagau vāsudevāya yat prokta tup manu yu mahiṣīṇā purā putra artha yaga vṛta kailāsam śaṃkara ālayam vasudev śrutaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ tapaḥ taptum śivasya hi atrā upamanyum saṃdṛṣṭā tapaṃtam śṛṅge uttame praṇamya bhaktyā sa muniḥ paryapṛcchat kṛtāñjiliḥ śrī kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca upamanyoḥ mahā prājña śaiva pravāram saṃstate śruhi śaṃkara māhātmyam sadānanda ram śṛṇe śṛṇu kṛṣṇa mahāśiva mahimānam maheśithuḥ tapastha usham śaṃkaram ca tadā yugāt parivāram samastam ca viṣṣa ādī namra ādikāt tribhiḥ śaiḥ śobhā manasa jala śukham aṃvyayam eka padam mahā dṛṣṭam saṃjvālaka baletūlaiḥ dvi sahastramī ukṣānām jyotiṣā asti ti varā ji tvam sahasrapād maheśvara bhuja uta sṛṣṭam trailokkyam sacarācaram nindet āha śrutakutsnam nimaṣādṛś na saṃśayaḥ rudra pārśva stham dṛṣṭavān imantam vijyā nimagham ati ugre sa veśa astra aṭṭa nāśakam dārayet yat mahīm kutsanām śoṣayet yat mahā dighim pātayet akhilam jyotiṣkam saṃśayaḥ yovāna aśaḥ hataḥ yena māṃdhātā sa balaḥ puṣā haihayasya niḥśiptaḥ lavaṇa asuraḥ śatrugum nṛpatīm yuddhe samāhūya samantataḥ tīkṣṇa agram saṃtrāsa jananam mahat viśikhān bhṛkuṭīm kṛtvā sthitam vipughām anala saṃkāśam bāla sūryam imā udditam sūryam stamin indreśtyam pāśa hastim avāntakam paraśum tīkṣṇa dhāram ca sarpa urvī īśa viśṛṅkhitam kalpa anta dahana ākāram tathā puruṣa vigraham tris sapta kṛtvas na kṣaram daṃdāha dviṣataḥ muniḥ sudarśanam tathā cakram sahasra vadanam viṣṇom dvidh sahasra bhujam devam drāk sam puruṣa ākṛtim dvidh sahasra bāhum dīptam sahasra caraṇa ākulam koṭi sūrya pratīkāśam trailokya dahana kṣamamāt vāñjam mahā udbhavam tīkṣṇam śata parvam anuttamam ā mahāghuḥ pinākam ca sātūṇīram mahā jutimā śaktim khaḍgam ca pāśam ca mahā dīptam samākuśam gadām ca mahatam divyām anvānya anyāṇi dṛṣṭavān tathā ca lokapālānām āstrāṇi etāni yāni ca adrākṣam tāni sarvāṇi bhagavat dru darśanataḥ vāma pārśve tu tasya eva śaṃkha cakra gadā gharaḥ vaiteyam samāsthāya tathā nārāyaṇaḥ sthitaḥ svāyaṃbhuva ādyāḥ manavaḥ bhṛgu ādyāḥ ṛṣayaḥ tathā śakra ādyāḥ devatāḥ ca eva sarve eva samam yayuḥ skandha śaktim samādāya devyāḥ samīpe saṃtasthau dvitīyaḥ iva pāvakaḥ nandī śūlam samādāya bhava gne samavasthitaḥ sa mātaraḥ vividhāḥ sthitāḥ teṣā abhivādya maheśānam parivārye samaṃtataḥ tat sarve bhagavat pārśve nirīkṣya aham su nirvismitaḥ su maheśvaryam ālaṃbya prāñjaliḥ vidviṣaiḥ stotaiḥ parama ānanda saṃmagnaḥ kṛṣṇa ahardare sammukhe śaṃkaram dṛṣṭvā bāṣpa gadgadayā girā apūjayam su viṣaya vat aham śraddhā sama anvitaḥ bhagavān atha su prīta śaṃkaraḥ parameśvaraḥ vācyā madhurāyā prītyā mām āha prahasan iva na vicālayitum śakyaḥ mayā vipra punar punar parīkṣita usite te bhavān bhakti anvitaḥ dṛḍhaḥ tasmāt te parituṣṭoṣmi varam varayā subrata sa ca aham tad bhavaḥ śrutvā śaṃboḥ sat premaṃyutam devam tam prāñjali bhūtvā anamam bhakta anukampinam tena satyena me jñānam tri kāla viṣayam bhavet prayaccha bhaktim vipulām ca anyabhicāriṇīm sa anvayasya api nityam me bhūriḥ kṣīrodanam evam uktaḥ māyā śaṃbhuḥ vindhasya parameśvaraḥ kṛpā dṛṣṭyā nirīkṣya āśu mām sa prāha yat ūdṛha śivaḥ uvāca upamanyo śṛṇu tāta vijñatas tvam bhaviṣyasi jarā maraṇa jaiḥ doṣaiḥ sarva kāma anvitaḥ bhava munīnām pūjanīyaḥ ca yaśaḥ avana samnvitaḥ śīla rūpa guṇa aiśvaryaiḥ mad prasādāt pade pade kṣīroda sāgarasya eva sānidhyam payasānidhiḥ amṛta ātmakam tat kṣīram yāvat saṃprāpyate tatas tvad bhoktram ca akṣyam ca astu mad prasādāt sadā eva hi sānidhyam āśrame te aham kariṣyāmi mahā śune ca astu sadā dāsyāmi darśanam yathākāma sukhām tiṣṭha na utkṇṭhām kartumaṃsi sarve yātu cintitam na atra saṃśayaḥ evam dṛṣṭaḥ mayā kṛṣṇa parivāra sam anvitaḥ śaṃkaraḥ parameśānaḥ mukti mukti pradāyakaḥ śaṃbhunā parameśena yat uktam tena dhīmatā pratyakṣam ca eva te jātānām gharva oṃ psaraḥ tathā ṛṣīṇām vidyādharān ca eva paśya siddhān vyavasthitān sarve mā etat mahā bāho śaṃkarasya mahātmanaḥ mama asti tu ikhilam jñānam prasādāt cūlapāṇinaḥ bhūtam bhavyam bhaviṣyam ca sarve jānāmi tattvataḥ tam ahām dṛṣṭvān devam api devāḥ sura īśvarāḥ ṣaḍviṃśakam iti khyātam param tattvam sanātanam sarve tattva vijñāna jñaḥ sarva tattva artha darśanaḥ saḥ eva bhagavān dṛvaḥ pradhāna puruṣa īśvaraḥ yaḥ nijāt ikṣiṇāt pāśān dṛhṇām loka kāraṇam vāma ādi asṛjat iṣṇum loka rakṣā artham īśvaraḥ kalpa ante ca eva saṃprāpte asṛjat ūrne hṛdaḥ prabhuḥ yugānte sarva bhūtāni saṃvatekartvā iva analaḥ kālaḥ bhūtvā mahādevaḥ asmānaḥ tasmin tiṣṭhati sarvajñaḥ sarva bhūta ātmā sarva bhūta bhodṛ bhavaḥ atas tvam putra laṃbhāya samārādhaya śaṃkaram śīghram prasannaḥ bhavitā bhakta vatsalaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe pañcamyām umāsaṃhitāyām kṛṣṇa upamanyu saṃvāde nāma prathamaḥ adhyāyaḥ jāta bhakti karme hādeve kṛṣṇaḥ provāca tam munim śrī kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca śune tāta kṛpām kuru mama upaḥ yeṣe śivam samārādhya kāmān āpuṣka tānvat sānatkumāraḥ uvāca iti ākṛṣṇyā upamantuḥ sa muni mahān kṛṣṇa vākyam śuprśasya pratyuvāca kṛpā nidhiḥ prāptaḥ hṛd kāma hi tān tān saktaḥ śṛṇu tvam vai yat ṛdṛha śarvāt savāmaiḥ eśvaryye hiraṇyakaśipuḥ purā vaṣāṇām daśa lakṣāṇi saḥ aḍala bhaṃdreśekharāt tasya ādyam putra a pravaraḥ nandanaḥ nāma viśrutaḥ viṣṇucakram ca tadroḥ vaḍamābhaṇḍalasya ca śīrṇī purā asaḥ abhavat kṛṣṇa tad aṃgeṣu mahā āhave na śastrāṇi vahanti aṃge dhīmataḥ su balīyasā śata vaṃrṣam sahasṣāṇi sampariḥ tathā putra sahasṣāṇām abhutam ca śivaḥ kuśadvīpe śubham rājyam addāt abhagavān prabhaḥ sa tasmai śaṃkaraḥ vāsudevam mahṛdghyaiḥ ghātrā śṛdya śata makhaḥ daityyaḥ vaṣa śatam purā tapaḥ kṛtvā sahasram tu putrāṇām alam abhravāt arādhya sa mahādevam prāptavān ajña anuttamam vedavyāsaḥ tu yaḥ nāmnā prāptavān tulam yaśaḥ saḥ api śaṃkaram ārādhya tri kāla jñānam āptavān indreṇa bālu vidhyāḥ te paribhūtāḥ tu śaṃkarāt lebhire garuḍam sa vaidurjeyeṣu āpaḥ avanaghāḥ sarvān ca pṛthvī ropāt kapa hidvanaḥ tṛīṇi vaṃśa śatāni ca muśleṣu nirāhārā kṣudhā śarvāt tatas stutān gaṃgām pravṛtyāmāsa citrakūṭe prativatā vikṛṇen ca mahādevam citrasenaḥ prasādya dṛḍha bhaktimān śrī karaḥ citrāṃgadaḥ patiḥ hare śivāt utprahataḥ maṃtraḥ yatunā ayam mṛtaḥ na hi sa ca takṣālam gatvā tad mitrām prāpya āśanātaḥ sva gṛham prītaḥ nāna dhana samanvṛtaḥ sīmintina priyā tasya soma vrata aparāyaṇā kṛṣṇaḥ lebhe saubhāgya auttamam ṛ gataḥ lobhāt kṛtadāra ākṛtiḥ chala caṃcukā puṃścalī duhā gokarṇa dvijataḥ purā śrutā varmekatham śambhoḥ bhaktyā prāpa parām gatim svara yantu gṛhītaḥ cañcuka āpitaḥ śrutvā śiva purāṇam ca sa sat gatim prāpa śāṃkarīm piṅgalā māṇikā khyātā madrarāḍhaḥ dvija aghamaḥ mahānanda abhighā kācid śreṣyā śiva pāda āratā dṛḍhāt paṇāt su prāsādi śivam lebhe ca sat gatim kaikeṭhī dvija bālā ca sādarāhā śiva ratā param hi śukham prāpa vimarṣaṇaḥ ca nṛpatiḥ śiva bhaktim vidhāya vai gatim lebhe parām kṛṣṇa śiva anugṛhītaḥ purā durjanaḥ ca nṛpaḥ pāpī khalaḥ śiva bhaktyā śivam prāpa nirliṃptaḥ saṃkīrṇeśvaraḥ nāmṇā śaṃkarasya śiva ratī saumini nāma cāṇḍālī saṃpūjya ajñānataḥ hi sā lebhe śaivīm gatim kṛṣṇa śaṃkara anugṛhāt parāt mahākāla abhighaḥ vyāghaḥ kirātaḥ parihiṃsakaḥ muni sādṛśa āliḥ śiva anugṛhītaḥ purā kauśikaḥ ca samārādhya śaṃkaram loka saṃkaram brāhmaṇa ūḍha trātriyaḥ ca dvitīyaḥ iva pūjyaḥ abhūt saṃgaṃkaraḥ kṛṣṇa sarva loka upitāmahaḥ śiva bhakta varāḥ śrīmān śiva anugṛhītaḥ hare śiva anugṛhītaḥ kṛṣṇa sarva deva adhipaḥ prabhuḥ bilipūtraḥ mahāśaivaḥ śiva anugṛhītaḥ vaśī bāṇaḥ babhūva brahmāṇḍa nāyakaḥ sakala īśvaraḥ hariḥ śaktiḥ ca sat gatyā dīrghicaḥ ca maheśvaraḥ śiva anugṛhīta ūḍha dhūrvaḥ tathā rāmaḥ hi śāṃkaraḥ kāṇādāḥ bhārgavaḥ ca evam gurugauṃtamaḥ eva ca śiva bhaktyāḥ babhūvuḥ te mahā prabhe īśvarāḥ śākalyaḥ śāṃsita ātmā ca nava varṣa śatāni api bhava māra abhyāyāsam manaḥ yajñena māghavaḥ akṣayam ca kulam teḍaḥ tu mahiṣibhiḥ araṃkṛtam bhaviṣyasi ṛṣi śreṣṭha sūtra kartā tatas tatas iti evam śaṃkarāt prāpa varam muni vara ṛstave trailokye vitata aśāsīḥ pūjyaḥ ca yadunandana sā avṛṇīḥ iti vikhyātam ṛṣiḥ āsīt kṛte yuge idam tena tapaḥ tāpam ṣaṣṭi varṣa śatāni ca tam āha bhagavān rudraḥ sākṣāt śughoṭ asmi teḍanagha evam viṣṇo mahādevaḥ puṇya puṣpa vairāḥ tatas samarcitam śubhān kāmān pradāti yathā īpsitān ekena eva mukhena āham vaktum sagavataḥ guṇāḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe pañcamyāḥ sumā saṃhitāyām sanatkumāra vyāsa saṃvāde upamanyupadeshaḥ nāma dvitīya ūḍha adhyāyaḥ sānatkumāraḥ uvāca evam śrutvā vacaḥ tasya saḥ aśravīt mahāśunimṛ vismayam paramam gatvā upamanyum śānta mānasam vāsudevaḥ uvāca yasya sāṃbhīm kurute śrame darśanam dadyāt bhagavān civaḥ api tāvat mama api evam prasādam vā karotu ayau aciṇā eva kālena mahādevam na saṃśayaḥ ṣoḍaśe māsi suvarān prāpyasi tvam maheśvarāt sa patnīkāt katham naḥ dāsyate devaḥ varān hare pūjyaḥ asi devataiḥ api sarvaiḥ chāghonīyaḥ sadā guṇaiḥ jāpyam te aham pravakṣyāmi śraddhānāya vā acyutam tena japa prabāveṇa satyam drakṣyasi śaṅkaram evam kathayataḥ taṃsya mahādeva āśritāḥ kathāḥ dināni adya prayātāni muhūrtāni iva tāpasaḥ mantram avyāpitam mahat jaṭī muṇḍī ca sadyas asau vabhuva suḥ samāhitaḥ saṃprāpte ṣoḍaśe māsi santuṣṭaḥ parameśvaraḥ kṛṣṇāya darśanam praṇatam ca viśeṣeṇa nānā bhūṣaṇa bhūṣitam sva aṃśraya mayam kāntam maheśrama jam avyayam nāna gaṇa anvitam tuṣṭam putrābhyām sthutam praśupam śrī kṛṣṇaḥ prāñjaliḥ hṛṣṭā vismaya utphulla uccanaḥ īdṛśam śaṃkaram prītaḥ praṇanāma mahā utsavaḥ nānāvidhaiḥ stuti parda evā aṃga mayena asamyak tadā sahasra nāmnā devaśam tuṣṭāva nata kandharaḥ tatas devāḥ sa gaṃdharvāḥ vidyādhara mahā urḍāḥ saṃmuttaḥ puṣpa vṛṣṭim ca sādhuvādāt manoganāt pārtyāśa mukham dṛṣṭvā bhagavān bhakta vatsalaḥ uvāca keśavam tuṣṭaḥ rudraśā atha mahādevaḥ uvāca kṛṣṇa jānāmi bhaktam tvam nityam daḍha vratam vṛṇīṣva tvam varān mattaḥ puṇya a trailokya dhulabhān tasya tat vacanam śrutvā kṛṣṇaḥ prāñjaliḥ ādravat prāha sarva īśvaram śaṃbhum su praṇamya punar punar kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca devadeva mahādeva yācet aham śuttamān varān tvad sāmīpyam sthirā bhaktiḥ tvāyi nityam mama astu iti putrāṇi ca daśa ānānam purāṇām mama santu vai vadhyāḥ ca ripavaḥ sarvaiḥ saṃgrāme bala dīptāḥ vaṣṭabhaḥ sarva aiśvaraḥ tvam mā iva asim mat praśuṃca viśeṣataḥ sarvaiḥ bhaviṣyati iti evam punar sa prāha śūladhṛk sāṃbaḥ nāma mahā vīryaḥ putaḥ te bhavitā balī māṇuṣe bhavitāsi iti sa te putraḥ bhaviṣyati evam labdhvā varān sarvān śīkṛṣṇaḥ parameśvarāt nānāvidhābhiḥ bhītimastutibhiḥ sam toṣayat tam āha atha śivā tuṣṭā pārvatī bhakta vatsalā vāsudavam mahātmānam śaṃśu bhaktam tapasvinam pārvatī uvāca vāsudeva mahā bhudhe kṛṣṇa tuṣṭā asmi gṛhāṇa matsva varān manoñjān suvi durlabhān iti ākarṇya vacaḥ tstastyāḥ pārvatyāḥ ca yat vṛṃhaḥ śrī kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca devi tvam paritūṣṭā asi ced dadāsi varān hi me tapasā anena satyena brāhmaṇān prīti mā asmabhūt kadācid hṛṣṭam tu pūjayetham dvijān sadā ca mātā pitarā mama sarvedā sarva bhūte ṣvāturkūlyam bhajeyam yatra tatragaḥ kule praśūtiḥ ucitā mama ārtu tava darśanāt tapeya ayam sura aindra ādīn daivāt yajña śatena tu yatīnām itīrthīnām ca sahasrāṇi atha sarvedā bhojayet sadā gehe śraddhā pūrvam tu bhojanam devi mā āryām saha bhaveyam prāṇa vallabhaḥ akṣīṇā kāṃbya tā tā āśu prasādāt tava śāṃkari āsām ca pitaraḥ loke bhaveyuḥ satyaṣāddinaḥ iti ādhāḥ prasādāt tava pāvāni evam asti iti bhaṃdhe te śāśvatī sarva kāma dā taiḥ smaḥ tān ca varān datvā pārvatī parameśvarau tat na eva antar ca daghatuḥ kṛtvā kṛṣṇasya satkṛpām kṛṣṇaḥ kṛtārtham ātmānam amnayat munī śvara upasmanyoḥ śunaiḥ āśu prāpa śramam atuttamam praṇamya śirasā tatra munim keśi hā tatas sa ca ta prāha vā añjana ahīn mahā dānapatiḥ loke koṃdhe vā asti iva duḥsadaḥ jñāne tapasi vā śauryem stheyam eva ca śṛṇu śaṃbhoḥ tu govinda daiva aiśvaryam mahā yaśāḥ tat śrutvā śraddhā yukta uṃsa vacam śaṃbhoḥ tu bhaktimān papraccha śiva māhātmyam sa tam prāha muni īśvaraḥ bhagavān śaṃkaraḥ pūrvam brahma loke mahātmanā stutaḥ nāma sahasreṇa daṇḍinā brahma yoginā sāṃkhyāḥ paṭhanti tat hī tam vistīrṇam ca nighaṇṭu vat duḥjñānam māṇuṣāṇām tu stotram tat sarva kāma dam śaṃkaram tvam gaccha kṛṣṇa gṛham sukhi bhaviṣyasi sadā śiva bhakta gaṇāmaṇīḥ iti uktam tam namaskṛtya vāsudevaḥ muni īśvaram manasā saṃsmaran śaṃsum keśavaḥ dvārakām yayau sanaṃtaumāraḥ uvāca evam kṛṣṇa samārādhya śaṃkaram loka śaṃkaram kṛtārtha uṃsphud muni śreṣṭha sarva aṃjeya uṃsa bhavat tathā tathā dāśarathi rāmiḥ śivam ārādhya bhaktitaḥ vijayī śivāt dvuḥśarām cāpam jñānam vai param tamam rāvaṇam sa gaṇam hatvā setum baddhvā ambasām nidhau sītām prāpya gṛham yātaḥ bubhuje nikhilām mahīṣu tathā ca bhāgaṇaḥ rāmaḥ tapasā viṣṇum nirīkṣya duḥkhitaḥ śiva ātta param kṣatriyeṇa taiṣṭam tīkṣṇam sa paraśum lebhe nidindh dāha ca tena tān jiḥ tatas kṛtavaḥ kṣatra aṃśa prasannāt parameśvarāt ajeyaḥ śāma arśā eva soḍhyā api tapasām nidhiḥ liṅgāt canarataḥ nityam daṃśyate siddha cāraṇaiḥ kalpa ante punar eva asau ṛṣibhiḥ sthānam eva apyati asitasya āvṛjaḥ pūrvaiḥ pīḍyā kṛtavān tapāḥ adharmye dharmam alaṃbhiṅgam ārādhya kāma dam cākṣuṣasya manoḥ putre mahastthale vasiṣṭha śāpāt durasamadaḥ daṇḍaka araṇye ekaḥ tasmāt mṛtyu mukha ākāraḥ gaṇaḥ mṛga śukha uṃsa bhavat ajara amaratām śāpam punar ca saḥ śaṃkareṇa kṛtaḥ śrītyā nityam lambhodarā tuṃgaḥ gārgyaḥ mokṣam ca śuve durlabham kāmacāri mahā kṣetram kālajñānam mahat dimam catuṣpādam sarasvatyāḥ pāra gatam ca śāśvatam na tulyam ca sahasram tu puṇyānām mad dadau śivaḥ vedavyāsam tu yogi indram putram tuṣṭaḥ pīnākadhṛk māṇḍavyaḥ śaṃkareṇa eva jīvam da tvā visarjitaḥ varṣāṇām daśa lakṣāṇi dariddraḥ brāhmaṇaḥ guraveṃśmani putram tu gālvam yaḥ ca pūrvam āsīt haśramī gṛhataḥ vā munīśālāyām bhikṣuḥ āyāti tad dṛham bhāryā uvāca yaḥ kaścid avaiyam yatas kadācid tithibhiḥ kaścid kṣudh tṛṣā śāma tarṣitaḥ tāḥ tuvāca te tam ca sā prāha bhaṭaḥ madīyaḥ tu sāṃpratam na ca daśyate saḥ ṛṣiḥ tāsu vāciṃca idam jñātvā divyena cakṣuṣā viśvāmitra abhyanujñātaḥ tad puṇyaḥ gālavaḥ tathā gṛham āgatya mātuḥ sa śrutvā śāpam su dāruṇam ārādhya śaṃkaram devam pūjām kṛtvā tu śāṃbhavīm gṛhāt asau viniṣkrānta saṃsmaraḥ śaṃkaram hṛdā atha tam tanayam dṛṣṭvā pitā tam prāha sa āśliṣam mahādeva prasādāt ca kṛtakṛtyaḥ asi ma kṛtārthaḥ dhanavān putravān śiva mṛtaḥ asi jīvitaḥ punar iti vaḥ kathitam areṣaḥ na aham śaktaḥ samāsatas vyāsāt vaktum śaṃbhoḥ ca guṇāḥ śeṣasya api na sukhāni syuḥ iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe pañcamyām umāsaṃhitāyām kṛṣṇa ādiśivabhaktoddhāraṇaśivamāhātmyavarṇanam nāma tṛtīyaḥ usi dhyāyaḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ tāta atāt mahābhāga dhanyaḥ tvam hi mahāmate adbhutā iyam kathā śaṃbhoḥ śrāvitā parama ukti dā punar hi kathām śaṃbhoḥ vyāsa praśna anusārataḥ sūtaḥ uvāca evam eva guroḥ yāsaḥ pṛṣṭavān saḥ ajam sanatkumāram sarvajñam śiva bhaktam muni īśvaram vyāsaḥ uvāca sanatkumāra sarvajña śrāvitā iyam śubhā kathā śaṃkarasya maheśasya nānā līlā vibhāriṇaḥ punar hi mahādeva mahimānam viśeṣataḥ śraddhā ca mahatī śrotum mama tāta pravartate māyayā jñānam āhṛtya nānā līlā vibhāriṇaḥ śṛṇu vyāsa mahābuddhe śāṃkarīm sukhām kathām yasyāḥ śravaṇa mātreṇa śive bhaktiḥ prajāyate parā mūrtiḥ brahma a viṣṇu aiśvara ātmikā liṃga aliṃga rūpiṇī devānām yonayaḥ ca agre mānuṣī navamī ca yā tiraścām yonayaḥ pañca bhavanti ye vam caturdaśa bhūtāḥ vā vartamānāḥ vā bhaviṣyāḥ ca eva sarvatas śivāt sarvaim pravartate līyante vṛddhim āgatāḥ gaṃdharvāṇām manuṣyāṇām anyeṣām vā api sarvatas bandhu mitram atha ācārya om rakṣeta āḥ nyaguruḥ vā bhrātā pitā mātā śivaḥ mataḥ śiva sarva mayaḥ puṃsām svayam vedyaḥ parātparaḥ tad māyā paramā divyā sarvatra vyāpinī śune tad hīnam jagat sarvam sa deva asura mānuṣam śiva māyā prabhāveṇa apubhūt ariḥ kāma mohitaḥ cakre bahu vāram muni īśvara pāpam cakāra duṣṭa ātmā śāpam prāpa muneḥ tadā kāma adhīnaḥ kṛtaḥ gatvā ca ūrttutaḥ jagatprāṇaḥ api garvena mohitaḥ śiva māyayā caṇḍaraśmiḥ tu mātaṇḍaḥ mohitaḥ śiva māyayā kāma ākulaḥ badhvā āśu dṛṣṭa arhī haya rūpa pṛthak candraḥ ca mohitaḥ śaṃbho māyayā kā ma saṅkulaḥ mohitau tau api śunī śiva māyā vimohitau urvāśī taruṇī dṛṣṭā caskambhaḥ abhaḥ babhūvatuḥ agastyaḥ varuṇā jātaḥ vaḍavā agni sambhūtaḥ dakṣasya mohita śaṃbhu māyayā brahmaṇaskṛtaḥ brahmā ca bahu vāram hi mohitaḥ śiva māyayā abhavat roktu kāmaḥ ca sva kṛta tāyām parāḥ tu ca cyavanaḥ api mahā yogī mohitaḥ śiva māyayā kaśyapaḥ śivam āyātaḥ mohitaḥ kāma saṅkulaḥ yayāce kanyakām mohāt dhanvanaḥ nṛpateḥ purā garuḍaḥ śāṇḍilkī kanyām netu kāma rasu mohitaḥ vijñātaḥ tu tayā saṃghaḥ dagdha pakṣaḥ babhūva ha vibhāṇḍakaḥ muniḥ nārī dṛṣṭā kāma vaśam gataḥ ṛkṣyaśṛṅga sutaḥ tarasya mṛgyām jātaḥ śiva ājñayā gautamasya asaḥ dṛṣṭvā śāradvatīm nagrām rarāma śubhitaḥ tayā retaḥ skandham dadhāra svam droṇyām ca eva sa tapasaḥ tasmāt kalaśā jātaḥ droṇa śastrabhṛtām varaḥ parāśaraḥ mahā yogī mohitaḥ śiva māyayā matsya udaryām ca cikrīḍe kumāryām dāśa kanyayā viśvāmitraḥ babhūva atha mohitaḥ śiva māyayā reme menakayā vyāsa vane kāma vaśam gataḥ visiṣṭena virogeṇa tu kṛtvā punar śiva prasādāt ca brāhmaṇaḥ abhūtasaḥ eva vai rāvaṇaḥ vaiśravāḥ kāmī babhūva śiva māyayā sītām jahre kṣubudhiḥ tu mohitaḥ mṛtyum āpa ca bṛhaspatiḥ cinvaraḥ mohitaḥ śiva māyayā sā avṛ patnyā vaśī reme bhardvājaḥ tatas abhavat iti māyā prabhāvaḥ hi śaṅkarasya mahātmanaḥ iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe paṃcamyā ākhumāsaṃhitāyām śivamāyāprabhāvavarṇanam nāma caturthaḥ adhyāyaḥ ye pāpa niratāḥ jīvāḥ mahā narka hetavaḥ ye pāpa niratāḥ jīvāḥ mahā narka hetavaḥ te samāsena kathyante sa avaghāna tayā śṛṇu akārya abhiniveśaḥ ca caturdham karma mānasam abhakṣya bhakṣaṇam hiṃsā mithyā kārya aniveśanam caturdham karma kāyikam ye dviṣanti mahādevam saṃsāra aṇavam tārakam su mahat pātakam teṣām niraya aṇva gāminām ye śiva nindā guru nindā śiva jñānasya dūṣaṇam harati ye ca pustakam pātakāni āhuḥ ananta phala dāni ṣaḍ na abhinandati ye dṛṣṭvā śiva pūjām prakalpitām na namanti cittam dṛṣṭvā śiva liṅgam stuvanti na yathteṣṭa ceṣṭāḥ niśśaṅkāḥ sthitāḥ ramanti ca upacāra vinikṛta āśiśvā agre guru sānnidhyau sthāna saṃskāra pūjām ca ye na kurvanti parveṣu vividha chāḥ gurūṇām ca karmaṇi oga vyavasthitāḥ ye tyajanti śiva ācāram śiva bhaktān dviṣanti ca a saṃpūjya śiva jñānam ye adhīyate likhanti ca a saṃskṛta pradeśeṣu yathecṣṭam svāpayanti ca yaḥ kurvanti atra pāpate aśucivān aśuci sthāne yaḥ śṛṇoti ca na karoti ca śuśrūṣām mām ca bhakti bhāvataḥ guru karmāṇi asāghyam yat tad indu peṣām karoti ca guru māntam śaktim ca videśam praṣṭhitam tathā vairibhiḥ pariṣṭutam vā yaḥ santyajati pāpa kṛt tat grāhyā putra mitrāṣu yaḥ śāvaṣṇām karoti ca evam mānta darśinaḥ su mahat pātakāni āhuḥ śiva nindā asmāni ca krodha alobhāḥ bhrayā dveṣāt brāhmaṇasya vadhe tu yaḥ brāhmaṇam yaḥ samāhūya da tvā yaśāt dāti ca udāsīnām sabhā madhye brahma hā sa prakīrtitaḥ ātmānam nayati ukta balāt gavām vṛṣa abhitrūtānām dvijānām guru puṣṭakam brahma hā atyā samam jñeyam pātakam na atra saṃśayaḥ aḍhī iti yaḥ dvijaḥ vedam brahma jñānam śiva ātmakam san tyāgaḥ pañcayajñānām surā pānasya tat samam pitṛ mātṛ parityāgaḥ kūṭa sākṣyam dvija anṛtam āmiṣam śiva bhaktānām abhakṣyasya ca makṣaṇam vane niraparaghānām prāṇinām ca apaghātanam gavām mārgam vane grāme yaiḥ agniḥ pradīyate iti pāpāni ghorāṇi brahmahatyā samāni ca dīna sarva sva haraṇam nara strī gaja vājinām go bhū rajata vastrāṇām amī ṣadhīnām rasasya ca candana agaru kaṣṭūrī paṭṭavāsasām vikrayaḥ tu avipattaḥ yaḥ kṛtaḥ jñānāt dvijātibhiḥ rūkmasateyasam smṛtam kanyānām vara yogyānām adānam sahasre vare kumārisāhasam ghora madhya pakṣī niṣevaṇam svarṇa ādyāḥ ca gamanam guru bhāryāyāḥ uśasam smṛtam mahā pāpāni ca uktāni śṛṇu tvam upapātakam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe pañcamyāḥ sumā saṃhitāyām mahāpātakavaṃrṇanam nāma pañcama adhyāyaḥ para dāra abhigamanam sādhu kanyāṣu dūṣaṇam śiva āśrama tarūṇām ca puṣpa ārāma vināśanam yaḥ pīḍām āśrama sthānām ācaret iṣpakām api kupya ghānya pa śusteyam apām vyāpāvanam tathā yajña ārāma taḍāgānām dārān patyasya vikrayam tīrtha yātrā apavāsānām vrata upenaya karmṇām strī ghanāni upajīvinaḥ strībhiḥ atyanta nijajīnātāḥ arakṣaṇam ca nārīṇām māyayā strī niṣevaṇam kālān gata apradānam ca dhānya vṛkṣa upaṣevanam nindīta āśca ghana ādānam paṇyānām kūṭa jīvanam viṣama ārya pajrāṇām satatam vṛṣavāhanam utsāṭana abhicāram ca ghānya ādānam bhiṣakkrayā jihvā kāma upabhoga arthe yaḥ ti āraṃbhaḥ su karmaṃśu mūlena hi āpakaḥ nityam veda jñāna ādikam ca yatam grāhi ādi vrata syāga śvānyācāri nishevaṇam asat chātra ādi gamanam śuṣka tarka avalambanam deva agni guru sādhuṇām nindyāḥ brāhmaṇasya ca pratyakṣam vā parokṣam vā rājñām maṇḍalinām api sva karma a tyāginaḥ ca ye duḥśīlāḥ nāstikāḥ pāpāḥ sadā vā asatya vādinaḥ parvaṃkāle divā vā apsu na evau paśu yoniṣu strī puruṣa saṃprāpte āśām cheda krayāḥ ca ye janasya apriya vaktāraḥ krūra samaya vedi nañ bhetā taḍāṃga kūpānām saṃkrayāṇām rasasya ca eka paktti sthā nānam ca pākam edam karoti yaḥ strī narāḥ pāpaiḥ upapātakinaḥ smṛtāḥ yuktāḥ śṛṇu tān tu bravīmi te ye go brāhmaṇa kanyānām svāmi mitra tapasvinām vināśayanti kāryāṇi te narāḥ nārakāḥ smṛtāḥ para dravya harāḥ nityam taula mithyā tusārakāḥ sevante tu dvijāśūdrām surām badhanti kāmataḥ ye krūrāḥ ye api hiṃsā priyāḥ narāḥ vṛtti arthe ye api kurvanti dāna yajña ādikāḥ kriyāḥ goṣṭha abhijala rasyāsu taru chāyā nageṣu ca tyajanti ye purīṣāṇi āvarāma āyataneṣu ca lañjā śrama prasādeṣu madya pāna rataḥ ca ye kūṭaka īli bhujaṅgāḥ ca raṃbhā anveṣaṇa tatparāḥ vaṃśa iṣṭakā śilā kāṣṭhaiḥ śūlaiḥ śaṅkubhiḥ eva ca kūṭaśāsana kartāraḥ kūṭa karma kriyā ratāḥ kūṭa pāka anrava jñānām kūṭa saṃvyavahāriṇaḥ ghanuṣaḥ śastra śalyānām kartā yaḥ kraya vikrayī bhṛtyeṣu paśūnām damanaḥ ca yaḥ mithyā pravadataḥ vācaḥ ākarṇayati yaḥ śanais svāmi mitra guru drohi māyāvī capala śṭhaḥ ye māyā putra mittrāṇi bāla vṛddh kakṣatūrān bubhukṣitān vṛthāpākasaḥ vijñeyaḥ brahma viduṣu garuhītaḥ ye tāḍayanti gām krūrāḥ damyante ṣuḍhuṣuḍhuḥ pīḍayanti vāhayanti ca yojayan akṛta āhārān vismṛcaṃti saṃyatān ye bhāra kṣatraḥ gātān goḥ vṛṣān ca kṣudhā āturān na pālayanti yatlena go ghāḥ te nārakāḥ smṛtāḥ vṛṣāṇām vṛṣaṇāni ye ca pāpiṣṭhāḥ gālayanti ca vāhayanti ca gām vandhyām mahānārakinaḥ narāḥ āśayā samanu prāptān kṣudh tṛṣṇā śrama kiśīntān atithīn ca tathā anāthān svatantrān gṛham āgatān agni bhilāṣān dīnān vā bāla vṛddha kṣatūrān na anukaṃpanti ye mūḍhāḥ te yānti naraka arṇavam gṛheṣu athā smaśāna ādiṣu bāṃgaevāḥ sukṛtam duṣkṛtam ca eva gacchantam anugacchaṃti nārakī syāt dvija āghāmaḥ śilpanaḥ vaidyāḥ hemakārāḥ ca nṛpabha jāḥ abhṛtakāḥ kṛta saṃyuktāḥ sarve te nārakāḥ smṛtāḥ yasya rājñaḥ prajāḥ rāṣṭre pacyante nareṣu saḥ ye dvijāḥ parigṛhṇanti nṛpasya anyāya vartanaḥ te prayānti tu coreṣu nareṣu na saṃśayaḥ pāradārika caurāṇām caṃḍānām vidyate tu agham rājñaḥ bhavati nityaśas caura vat paśyet śorem vā acaurem rūpiṇam a vicārye nṛpaḥ tasmāt dāta yaṇa rakam vrajet madhu māṃsa surā āsavam guḍa ikṣu śāka dugdhāni dīrgha mūla phalāni ca tṛṇam kāṣṭha patra pu ṣpam auṣadham ca ātma bhojanam upānah chatra śakaṭa māsanam ca kamaṇḍalum tāmra sīsa trapuḥ śaṅkham śaṅkha ādyam ca jalodbhavam vaidyam ca vaiṇavam ca anyat dvi aṣṭa upakaraṇāni ca auṇṇaka āpāsa kauśeya paṭṭasūtra udbhavāni ca sthūla sūkṣmāṇi vastrāṇi ye lobhāt ca haranti ca evamādīni ca anyāni dravyāṇi vividhāni ca apahrtyā narāḥ yānti narakam na atra saṃśayaḥ śarīra yātna athāya sarvākāram avāśuyāt yama loke vrajanti ete śarīreṇa yama ājñayā sthitāḥ deva tīrthaiḥ manurṣyāṇām agham nirātmanām dharma rājaḥ smṛtaḥ śāstā sudhoreḥ iva vividhaiḥ niyama ācāra cyutānām pramāda āra rakhalita ātmanām prāyaścitteṣu śāstā na budhaiḥ jñāyate yamaḥ pāradārika caurāṇām anvāya vyavahāriṇām nṛpatiḥ śāsakaḥ proktaḥ pracchannānām sa dharmarāj tasmāt kṛtasya pāpasya prāyaścittam samācaret na abhyuktasya anyathā nāśaḥ kalpa koti śataiḥ api kāyena manasā vācā tasya pāpa gatiḥ phalam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe paścamyāhumāsaṃhitāyām pāpasevadvarṇanam nāma ṣaṣṭhaḥ adhyāyaḥ saṃsāra jananām ghoram strī puṃpuṃsaiḥ kaiḥ jinaiḥ jñātavyam sarva jantuṣu śubha aśubha phalam ca atra dehinām saṃvicāryate avaśyam hi kṛtam karma bhoktavyam tat icchā api etām tatra ye śubha karmāṇaḥ somya cittāḥ dayāvitāḥ ye punar pāpa karmāṇaḥ pāpāḥ dāna vivarjitāḥ te ghoreṇa pathā yānti dakṣiṇena yama ālayam ṣaṣ aśīti sahasrāṇi yojanānām ā atītya tat vaivasvatam puram jñeyam nānā rūpam avāsthitam narāṇām puṇya karmāṇām tīkṣṇa kaṇṭaka yuktena śarkarā vicitena ca kṣura ādhāra ānibhaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ pāṣāṇaiḥ racitena ca kvacid paśkena mahatā ukrāṇaiḥ ca pātakaiḥ loha śūcī nibhaiḥ daṃśaiḥ sampannena pathā kvacid taṭa prāyā ati viṣamaiḥ parvvataiḥ vṛkṣa saṅkulaiḥ pratat sa aṅgāra yuktena yānti mārggeṇa duḥkhitāḥ kaścid viṣama gartaiḥ ca kaścid śīṭa su duṣkaraiḥ śruta tvāḷukābhiḥ ca tathā tīkṣṇaiḥ ca śaṅkubhiḥ kvacid kaṣṭena tamasā mārge na an ālambet kvacid ayaḥ śṛṅgāṭakaiḥ stīkṣṇaiḥ kvacid adhāmnā punar kvacid ḍāḷukayā vyāpta makṭha antar praveśayā kvacid ḍaṃbunā vyāptam kvid ca kiraṣa agninā kvācid cīndaiḥ vṛkaiḥ vyaḥ agnaiḥ maśakaiḥ ca su dāruṇaiḥ kvācid mahā jalaukābhiḥ tathā makṣikābhiḥ ca raudrābhiḥ kvicat sarpaiḥ viṣa ulbvaṇaiḥ matta mātaṅga yūthaiḥ ca bala unmattaiḥ pramāthibhiḥ śūkaraiḥ tīkṣṇa daṃṣṭibhiḥ tīkṣṇa śṛṅgaiḥ ca mahiṣaiḥ sarvva bhūtaiḥ śyāpadaiḥ ḍākinībhiḥ ca raudrābhiḥ vikārālaiḥ ca rākṣasaiḥ vyāḍhibhiḥ ca mahā coraiḥ pīḍyamānāḥ vrajanti hi mahāgūḍilivimiśreṇa mahācaṇḍena vāyunā mahā pāṣāṇa varṣeṇa hvanyamānāḥ nirāśrayāḥ mahatā vāṇa varṣeṇa vidhyamānāḥ ca sarvvatas pati dvi veṣa pātaiḥ ca ulkā pātaiḥ ca dāruṇaiḥ pradīpta aṅgāra varṣeṇa dahyamānāḥ ca santi hi mahatā pāṃśu varṣeṇa pūryamāṇāḥ rudanti ca mahā megha varaiḥ coraiḥ ca syante ca śuḍuḍuḍuḥ niśita āyudha varṣeṇa bhidyamānāḥ ca sarvvatas mahā śārā aṃbu pārābhiḥ sacyamānāḥ vrajanti ca mahā śītena marutā rūkṣeṇa paruṣeṇa ca samantāt ḍādhyamānāḥ ca śuṣyante saṅkucanti ca viṣameṇa eva mahatā nirjana apāśrayeṇa ca tamaḥ kleśena kaṣṭena sarvva dugdha āśrayeṇa ca nīyante dehinaḥ sarve ye mūḍhāḥ pāpa kārmiṇaḥ yat dūtaiḥ ma ha aghoraiḥ tat ajñā kāribhiḥ balāt ekākinaḥ para adhīnāḥ mitra bandhu vivarjjitāḥ karmāṇi rudantaḥ ca śuḍuḍuḥ pretāḥ bhūtvā vivikṣāḥ ca śuṣk kaṇṭha oṣṭa tālukāḥ asomyāḥ bhavati itāḥ ca dahyamānāḥ kṣudhā anvitāḥ baddha āśṛṅkhalayā kecid uttāna pādakāḥ narāḥ kṛṣyante kṛṣyamāṇāḥ ca yam dūtaiḥ bāla utkaṭaiḥ vṛṣyamāṇāḥ tu duḥkhitāḥ keśa pāśa nibanddhena saṃkṛṣyante ca rajjunā laḷāṭe ca aṅkuśena anye duṣyanti dehnaḥ uttānāḥ kvicid aṅgāra vartmanā paścāt āhu nibaddhāḥ ca jaṭhareṇa prapīḍitāḥ pṛthitā śṛṅkhalābhiḥ ca hastayoḥ su kīlitāḥ grīvā pāśena kṛṣyante prayānti anye su duḥkhitāḥ jihvā aṅkuśa praveśena rajjvā aṅkuṣyan eva te nāsā bhedena ruvā ca tu āṅkuṣyante tathā apare bhinṇāḥ kapōlayoḥ rajjvā aṅkṛṣyante oye tathā uṣṭayoḥ karṇa uṣṭha nāsikāḥ sañchinna a śiśna vṛṣaṇāḥ chinna bhinna aṅga saṃghayaḥ ābhidyamānāḥ kuṇṭaiḥ ca bhindhyamānāḥ ca sāyakaiḥ itas ca itas ca dhāvantaḥ krandamānāḥ nirāśrayāḥ mudraiḥ loha daṇḍaiḥ ca hanyamānāḥ su duḥkhitāḥ śaktāku kimi dagdhāḥ ca nīyante vivaśāḥ narāḥ yācamānāḥ ca salilam antam vā api bubhukṣitāḥ chāyām prārthayamānāḥ ca śīta ārtiśa analam punar dāna ahīnāḥ prayānti evam prārthayantaḥ sukham narāḥ gṛhīta dāna pathaiyāḥ sukham yānti yama ālayam evam nyāyena kaṣṭena prāptāḥ preta puram yadā prajñāpitāḥ tatas dūtaiḥ niviśyante yama agratas tatra ye śubha karmāṇaḥ tān tu samnānayet yamaḥ svāgata āsan dānena ā pādya arghyeṇa priyeṇa ca dhanyāḥ yūyam mahātmānaḥ nigama utpādita kāriṇaḥ divyam vimānaya āruḍhya divya bhoga upaśitāṣu tatra muktāḥ mahā bhoga ante puṇyasya saṃkṣayāt dharma ātmānaḥ narāḥ ye ca mitrabhtāḥ iva ātmanaḥ ye punar krūra karmāṇaḥ te paśyanti bhayānakam daṃṣṭrā karāla vadanam śikuṭī kuṭila īkṣaṇam ūrdhva keśam mahā śmaśru yuktham praghurita adharam aṣṭādaśa bhujam kruddhan nīlāñjana caya upamam sarva āyudha āḍhṛta karam sarva daṇḍena mahā mahiṣa āroḍham dīpta agni sama lochanam samīpa sthāḥ kāla anala sama prasaḥ kāla śmāśā añjana saṃkāśāḥ kṛtāṃtaḥ ca bhayānakāḥ mārī ca ugra mahā mārī kālarātriḥ ca dāruṇā vividhāḥ vyāghrayaḥ kuṣṭhāḥ nānā rūpāḥ bhaya āvahāḥ śakti śūla aṅkuśa dharāḥ ca kāsi pāṇayaḥ vajra tuṇḍa dharāḥ rudrāḥ kṣura tīkṣṇa ghanu ghnṛāḥ nānā āyudha gharāḥ sarve mahā vīrāḥ bhayaṃkarāḥ asaṃkhyātāḥ mahā vīrāḥ kālāgni samprabāḥ sarva āyu ghora karāḥ yamadūtāḥ bhayānakāḥ anena paricāreṇa vṛtam tam ghora darśanam yam paśyanti pāpiṣṭhāḥ ca śrutam ca bhīṣaṇam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe pañcamyām umāsaṃhitāyām narakalokamārgaṃyadūtasvarūpavaṇanam nāma saptamaḥ adhyāyaḥ mo mo duṣkṛta karmāṇaḥ para dravya apahārakāḥ garvitā rūpa vīryeṇa para dārava mahñkāḥ tat kim ātma upacāta arthe bhaviṣya duṣkṛtam kṛtam idānīm kim pralapsyāmce pīḍyamānāḥ sva karmabhiḥ bhuñjyantām svāni karmāṇi na asti doṣaḥ hi kasyacid evam te pṛthivīpālāḥ saṃgrāhāḥ tad samīpatas svakīyaiḥ karmabhiḥ ca eraiḥ duṣkarmā imbalda pīṇaḥ saṃśikṣayati dharma jñaḥ yama rāja anuśikṣayā bho bho nṛpāḥ durācārāḥ prajā abhighna sākāriṇaḥ alpa kālasya rājyasya kṛte kim duṣkṛtam kṛtam rājya bhogeṇa mohena balāt anyāyataḥ prajāḥ yat iṇḍatāḥ phalam tasya bhuñjatām adhunā nṛpāḥ tat svaim saṃparityajya yūyam ekākiṇaḥ sthitāḥ paśyāmi tat vulam naṣṭam yena vighna sitāḥ prajāḥ adhunā kīdṛśam bhavet svāni karmāṇi śocanti tūṣṇīm tiṣṭhanti pārthivāḥ iti karmani samuddiśya nṛpāṇām dharmara ādayaḥ tad pāpa pṅkśuddha ṛdhyasmi idam dūtān bravīti ca yamarājaḥ uvāca bho bhoṣaṇḍa mahā caṇḍa gṛhītvā nṛpatīn balāt niyamena viśuddha cakṣvam krameṇa naraka aṃniṣu tatas śīghram samādāya nṛpān saṃgṛhya pādayoḥ tu vegeṇa nikṣipya ucṣai praṣṭhā ca sarveṇa mahatā atīva tase śilā tale āsphālayanti tarasā vajreṇa iva mahā āṭumān tatas sraktam śroṇeṇa sravate jarjarīkṛtaḥ niḥsaṃjñaḥ tu tadā dehī tatas sa vāyunā spṛṣṭaḥ stu taiḥ ujjīvitaḥ punar tatas pāpa aviśuddhi arthe kṣipanti naraka aṇave aṣṭāviṃśati saṃkhyābhiḥ kṣiti aghasata koṭayaḥ ghora ākhyā prathamā koṭiḥ su ghorā tad ghas sthitā atighorā mahāghorā ghorarūpā ca pañcamī ṣaṣṭī talāt lākhyā ca saptamī ca bhayaṃkā aṣṭamī kālarātriḥ ca navamī ca bhaya utkṭā daśamī tad ghaṣaṇḍā mahācaṇḍā tatas apyaḥ caṇḍakolāhalā ca anyā pracaṇḍā caṇḍanāyikā karālā vikarālā ca vajrā viṃśatimā smṛtā tri koṇā pañca koṇā ca su dīrghā ca akhilā atindā samā bhīma balamā uṣṇā dīpta prāyā iti ca aṣṭamī iti te nāmataḥ proktāḥ ghorāḥ naraka koṭayaḥ aṣṭāviṃśatiḥ eva ettāḥ pāpānām yātanā ātmikāḥ tāsām krameṇa vijñeyāḥ pañca pañca eva nāyakāḥ pratyekam sarva koṭīnām nāmataḥ san nibodhata tatas tathā ca uṣṇam pañca adhā nāthakāḥ smṛtāḥ sūca urasṭha mahā tīkṣṇaḥ tayā saṃjīvanaḥ smṛtaḥ mahātamaḥ vilomaḥ ca vilopāśvā api kaṇṭakaḥ tīvravegaḥ karālaḥ ca vikrālaḥ prakampanaḥ mahāvakraḥ ca kālaḥ ca kālasūtraḥ pragaḍajaḥ sūcīmukha sthānetiḥ ca kṣādakra sthāma pīḍanaḥ bherā uda asṛj prahitaḥ tatas tīkṣṇatuṇḍaḥ ca śakuni mahāsaṃtāṅkaḥ kathuḥ ucchvāsasmuniḥ ucchvāsaḥ rudīrgheḥ kūṭaśālmaliḥ duriṣṭa sthū mahā vādaḥ pravāhi sthū pratāpanaḥ tatas meghaḥ gṛṣaḥ śālmali sahasti āra gajānanāḥ śyaghuka rājam diṣaghra kokavṛka ānanāḥ śākhu nimīna nakākhyā salpa kumāriya vāyasāḥ gṛśa ulūka haliñkāryāḥ śārdūla kṛtha kāṭāḥ yandukāḥ putivakāḥ aśa rakṣāsaḥ pūtiputrikāḥ tathā agnīḥ ca rudhirābha śvabhojanaḥ ca sarve amkṣaḥ su dāruṇaḥ vikaṭaḥ kaṭapūtanaḥ ambārīṣaḥ kaṭāhaḥ ca kaṭhā vaitaraṇī nadī eka pādaḥ praphūraṇaḥ asitāla vanam ghoram asthi abhaṅgaḥ śupūraṇaḥ vilātasoḥ tu yantrāṇi api kūṭapāśāḥ pramardanaḥ tapta loha mayam tathā parvataḥ kṣurādhārā ca tathā yamala parvataḥ sūtraviyāśaṅkupaḥ ca kṣārakūpaḥ ca śītalaḥ ghuṣa lotrūkhalam yantram śilā śakaṭa lāṅgalam mahā śakaṭa maṇḍapam bahu duḥkham mahā kleśāḥ kaśmalam sa malam malāt hālāhalaḥ virūpaḥ ca svaropaḥ ca yamānugaḥ eka pāda dvi pādaḥ ca tīvra aśa cīvaram tamaḥ aṣṭāviṃśatiḥ iti ete kramaśas koṭīnām ānupūrvyeṇa pañca pañca eva nāyakāḥ rauravāya prabodhyante narakāṇām śatam smṛtam proktam mahānaraka maṇḍalam prasaṃkhyānaḥ ca vairāgyam śṛṇu pāpa gatim ca tām iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe pañcamyām umāsaṃhitāyām narakalokavarṇanam nāma aṣṭamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śṛṇu pāpāḥ prapaṃcyante śoṣyante naraka agniṣu yātnābhiḥ vinicitrābhiḥ ā sva karma prekṣayā dṛśam tatra pāpa kṣata apāpāḥ narāḥ kṛmīkura upatāḥ su gādham hastayoḥ baddhā tatas śṛṅkalayā narāḥ mahā vṛkṣam śākhāsu lambhyante yama kiṅkaraiḥ dolī antar ca ativegena visaṃjñāḥ yānti yojanam antarikṣa sthitānām ca loha bhāra śatam punar teṣām yamadūteḥ mahā balaiḥ tena bhāreṇa mahatā prabhṛśam tāḍitāḥ narāḥ dhyāyanti svāni karmāṇi tūṣṇīm tiṣṭhanti niḥśvalaḥ tatas udaṃkuśaiḥ agni variṇaiḥ lohā daṇḍaiḥ ca dāruṇaiḥ hanyante kiṃkaraiḥ ghoraiḥ saṃmantāt pāpa kṛmmiṇaḥ tatas kṣāreṇa dīptena bahvoḥ api viśeṣataḥ drutena atyanta liṅgena kṛtta aṅgāḥ jarjarīkṛtāḥ punar ivda arcye ca aṅgāni śirasaḥ prabhṛti kamāt viṣṭhā pūrṇe tathā kūpe kṛmīṇām nicaye punar medaḥ asṛj pūya pūrṇāyām vāpyām kṣipyanti te punar bhakṣyante kṛmibhiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ lohituṇḍaiḥ ca vāyasaiḥ śibhiḥ daṃśaiḥ vakaiḥ ca anyaiḥ raudraiḥ ca vikṛta ānanaiḥ pacyante matsya vat śā api pradīpta aṅgarā rāśiṣu bhinnaḥ śūlaiḥ su tīkṣṇaiḥ ca narāḥ pāpena karmaṇā tilāḥ iva prapīḍyante cakrāṇi ye taila pūrṇa kaṭāheṣu śuntateṣu punar punar bahudhā pacyate jihvā prapīḍacyā urasīn pādayoḥ yātanāḥ ca mahatyaḥ śarīrasya ati sarvatas niḥśeṣa narkebhyaḥ api kramantiśas narāḥ yāmyaiḥ ca drīyate vyāsa sarva aṅgeṣu sukhaṣadā jvalat aṅgāram ādāya mukham ā āpūrya tāḍyate tatas kṣāreṇa dīptena tāmreṇa ca punar punar itas tatas pīḍayitvā bhṛśam āpūrya hanyate viṣṭhābhiḥ kṛmibhiḥ ca api pūryamāṇāḥ kiñcid kinñcid pariṣvajanti ca ati ugrām pradīptām loha śālmalīm hanyante pṛṣṭha deśe ca punar dīptyoḥ mendhāgavaiḥ śiraḥ prabhṛti pīḍyante karmobhiḥ ātmajaiḥ khādyante ca sva māṃsāni pīyate śoṇitam svakam annam pānam na dattam yaiḥ sarvadā sva ātma poṣakaiḥ ikṣu vat te prapīḍyante jarjarīkṛtya mudraiḥ sūcībhiḥ bhinna sarva aṅgāḥ tatas śūla āropitāḥ saṃcālyamānāḥ bahuśas kruśyante na mriyanti ca tathā ca tad śarīrāṇi suṣa duḥkha sahāni ca dehāt utpāṭya māṃsāni bhidyante svaiḥ ca mudraiḥ nirghrāṇe narake ciram uttāḍyante tathā ugrāṇe vāḍukā sadane narāḥ mahāraurava pīḍābhiḥ meha antar api rudanti ca nikhanyante ghanaḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ su tamraiḥ loha śaṃkubhiḥ tu su duḥkhubhaḥ jantu paṅke bhṛśam tat te kṣiptāḥ krandanti visvaram pāpinaḥ krūra karmāṇaḥ sarvathā punar lālā bhakṣeṣu pāpāḥ te pātyante duḥkheṣu vai nānā sthāneṣu ca tathā narakeṣu punar punar sūcīmukhe mahā kleśe narake pātyate naraḥ pāpī puṇya vihīnaḥ ca tāḍyate yama arcikaiḥ aiḥ loha kumbhe viniḥkṣiptāḥ śvasantaḥ ca śanais śanais mahā agninā prapacyante sva pāpaiḥ eva mānavāḥ daḍham raju ādibhiḥ baddhā prapīḍyante śilāsu ca śiṣyante ca aṅgkuśeṣu dṛśyante amaraiḥ trī śadhū kṛmi bhiga abhirṇ rasa vargāḥ śataśas jarjarī kṛtāḥ su tīkṣṇa śāra kūpeṣu kṣipyante tad anantaram mahā jvāleṣu narake pāpāḥ krandanti duḥkhitāḥ ita śvetaḥ ca ghāvanti daḍhyamānāḥ tadārṣīṣā pṛṣṭhe ca ānīya tuṇḍābhyām vinyasta skaṅgha yojite tayoḥ madhyena vā ākuśya śāḍu pṛṣṭhena gāḍhataḥ baddhāḥ parasparam sarvāḥ su bhrūśam pāpa raṇa ābhaḥ baḍipuṇḍāraḥ tu darśyante mahājvāle tu yātanāḥ pāliṣṇāḥ kaddhaṣeṇa ca su tīkṣṇam cāritāḥ te hi karkeśāsu śilāsu ca āsphāla śataśas pāpāḥ pacyante tṛṇa vat tatas śarīra abhyantara gataiḥ prabhūtaiḥ kṛmibhiḥ nārāḥ bhakṣyante tīkṣṇa vadanaiḥ ātma dehaḥ kṣaya ādṛśam kṛmīṇām niñcaye kṣiptāḥ pūya maṃsa asthi rāśiṣu tiṣṭha pavetābhyām nipīḍitāḥ tātapyante vadanātaḥ pravinyastām kṣupra tapām ayoga dām te khādanti para adhīnāḥ taiḥ taḍcante saṣṭhūraiḥ varṇayāmi vivaraṇam teṣām tarkavāya karmiṇām iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe paṃcyāstumāsaṃhitāyām sāmānyatas narakagativṛṇaṃnam nāma navamaḥ adhyāyaḥ jihvāt dhīkoṣa vistīrṇaṃhūleḥ tīkṣṇaḥ prapīḍyate viṣṭhābhiḥ kṛmi mīśrābhiḥ ṣuṃvapṛtyam hinyate ye kāmāya udṛtana abhyaṃgam snāna pānān bhujanam krīḍanam maiṭhunam dyūtam ācarintam doḍha tāḥ vividhaiḥ caṃraiḥ kṣu yaṃtra ādi pīḍanaiḥ niryāmiṣu pacyante yāvat āhṛta saṃpluvam tena tena iva rūpeṇa tāḍyante pāradārikāḥ gāḍham āligya te nārīm clutanām lohinimūtām pūrva ākārāḥ ca puruṣāḥ prajvalanti samantataḥ duṣṭha ariṇīm khiyam gāḍham āliṅganti rudanti ca ye śṛṇvanti satām nindām teṣām karṇa praghūraṇam agni varṇaiḥ yaḥ kīleḥ taiḥ asta śrādiṃnimittaiḥ tṛpu sīsa ārakūṭa ādibhiḥ kṣīreṇa ca punar punar su tat tīkṣṇa tailena vajra lepeṇa vā punar karmāt āpṛtyam karṇoḥ tu narakaṣu ca yātanāḥ anukrameṇa sarvaiṃbhavantiyātāḥ samantataḥ sarva indrayāṇām api evam karmāt pāpena yātanāḥ bhavanti ghorāḥ pratyekam śarīreṇa kṛtena ca sparśa doṣeṇa ye mūḍhāḥ spṛśanti ca paribhrayam ateṣām kara uṣibhiḥ vāṇobhiḥ pāśubhiḥ pṛcyate bhṛśam teṣām kṣāra ādi biraḥ sarvaiḥ śarīram anulipyate yātanāḥ ca mahā kṣhaṭāḥ sarva eṣu narakaṣu ca śāṇi ye narāḥ vakāṇi teṣām sa antāni kīryante śaṅkubhiḥ dṛḍham para dārān ca paśyanti lubdhāḥ tastabhyena cakṣuṣā sūcībhiḥ śālim teṣām netra prapūraṇam kṣāradyaiḥ ca kramāt sarvāṃ ihāiva yamayatanāḥ bhavanti muni śārdūla satyam satyam na saṃśayaḥ loha kīla śataiḥ taiḥ tān tad jihvā āsyam ca pūryante ye deva ārām puṣpāṇi lobhāt saṃgṛhya pāṇinā jighrati ca narāḥ bhūyas śirasā dhārayanti ca āpūryante śiraḥ teṣām śaṅkubhiḥ nāsikā vāta vahulaiḥ tatas kṣāra ādibhiḥ bhrṣam ye nindanti mahātmānam vācakam dharma deśikam devāmi gurum uktān ca dharma śāstrām ca śāśvatam teṣām kaṇṭhe ca jihvāyām tāḍuni oṣṭhe nāsikāyām mūrdhni tad mānaḥ ca tri śākhāḥ loha āśaṅkavaḥ āvidhyante ca bahuśas sthāneṣu bheṣu kṣudraraiḥ tatas kṣāreṇa dīptena pūryante hi samantataḥ yātanāḥ ca mahantyaḥ vai sarvatas ye gṛhṇanti para dravyam paṇyām vipram spṛśanti ca śiva upakeraṇam gām ca jñāna ādibhiḥ likhitam ca yat hasta pada ādibhiḥ teṣām āpūryate samantataḥ na ṛkkeṣu ca sarveṣu vicitrāḥ dehayātanāḥ bhavanti bahuśas kaṣṭāḥ pāṇi pādaḥ samudravāḥ śiva āyatanam paśyante deva ārāmeṣu kutracid sadyas smṛjanti ye pāpāḥ purīṣam mūtram eva ca teṣām sa tṛṣṇam cūryante loha kṣudraiḥ sūcībhiḥ agni vaṇānibhiḥ tathā tlāghyante punar tatas kṣāreṇa mahatā tīvreṇa ca punar punar drutena pūryante gāḍham gude śirśane ca dehinaḥ indriyāṇām ca duḥkham prajāyate dhane sati api ye dānam na prayacchanti tṛṣṇayā atithim ca anvamanyante kāle prāpte gṛhāśrame tasmāt duṣkṛtam prāpya gacchanti narakāḥ śucau yeṣām da tvā hi bhuñjanti na sva bhayaḥ saha vāyasaiḥ teṣām ca vidrutam vakram kīlakadya tāḍitam kākinibhiḥ prāṇibhiḥ ca śailonhaṭuṇḍaiḥ ca vāyasaiḥ śyāmaḥ ca śabalaḥ ca eva yama dūta anurodhakau yaḥ stau taḥ tābhyām prayacchāmi tau gṛhītvā imam bilam ye vā varuṇa vāyavyāḥ yāmyāḥ naiṛtya vāyasāḥ vāyasāḥ puṇya karmāṇaḥ te praghṛhṇantu me bilam maṇḍalam tu kṛtvā gandha ādi vāsitam dhanvantari athā mīśānyā prācyām indrāya nikṣipet yāmyām yamāya vāruṇyām sudakṣomāya dakṣiṇe pitṛbhyaḥ tu viniḥkṣipya prācyām aryamaṇa tatas ghātubhiḥ eva vidhātuḥ ca dvār deśe viniḥkṣipet devaiḥ pitṛ manuṣyaiḥ ca pretaiḥ bhūtaiḥ sa vayobhiḥ kṛimi kīṭaiḥ ca gṛihasthaḥ ca upajīvyate svādhākāraḥ svabhākāraḥ vaṣaṭkāraḥ tṛitīyakaḥ iṃkāraḥ tathā eva ānyaḥ stana catuṣṭayam svāhākāram stane devāḥ svabhām ca pitaraḥ tathā vaṣṭkāram tathā iva anye devāḥ bhūta īśvarāḥ tathā iṃtakāram manuṣyāḥ ca pibanti satatam stanam yaḥ tetatāt manavaḥ śraddhayā jhanurṣīṣikām yaḥ tam jahāti vā svastaḥ tām iṣṭe sa tu majjati samyak eka kṣāmi nivāsinām sa tasmai duṣkṛitam dattvā puṇyam ādāya gacchati priyam eva aśan naraḥ śṛṃkhalabān punar yatas tam tila mātra prāmaṇataḥ dīyate teṣām bhittvā ca eva tu śoṇitam niḥśeṣataḥ kaśābhiḥ tu pīḍyate kramaśas punar bubhukṣayā antika gham hi tathā ca ati pipāsayā evamādhāḥ mahā ghorāḥ yātanāḥ pāpa karmṇām ante yat pratipad hi tat sakṣepeṇa śṛṃṇu dharme gurutaram vā api tathā āvṛitye tayoḥ śṛṃṇu pumān yaḥ sa upavāsaḥ yathā vittavān vijānāti pīḍām niyama saṃsthitaḥ tāni pāpāni ghorāṇi sānti yeṣām naraḥ śuvi iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe pañcamyā śumāsaṃhitāyām narakagatibhogavarṇanam nāma daśamaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca kuta pāpāḥ narāḥ yānti duḥkhena mahatā anvitāḥ avaśyam hi kṛitam karma śubha aśubham atas vakṣye tān dharmān sukha ādāyakān atra ye śubha karmāṇaḥ saumya cittāḥ dayā anvitāḥ yaḥ pradyāt sa naroāśvena mahatā sukham yāti yama ālayam śibikāyāḥ pradānena tanmathena sukham vrajet śayyā āsana pradānena sukham yāti su vidhrāmam āramat cāyāka tārī mārge vā vṛikṣa ropakāḥ yānti puṣpaka yānena puṣpa ārāma kara narāḥ devāyatana kartāraḥ krīḍanti ca guhodeśre kartāran ca tathā ye ca yatīnām ca anātha maṇḍapānām tu krīḍanti ca guhodeśre deva agni guru visrāṇām mātā pitroḥ ca pūjakāḥ pūjyamānā narā yānti kā aṃśukena yathāsukham dyotayantaḥ diśaḥ sarvāḥ yānti dīpa pradāyinaḥ pratiśraya pradānena mukham yānti nirāmayāḥ viśrāmyamāṇāḥ gacchanti guru śuśrūṣakāḥ narāḥ ātoḍya vipradātāraḥ sukham yānti svake gṛhe atra dattā atra pānāni tāni āpnoti naraḥ pathi pāda abhyaṅgam ca yaḥ kuryāt śat pūjena gacchati pāda śaucam tathā abhyaṅgam dīpa maṇam pratiśrayam raupyān duṣpradānena yama lokām sukhena saḥ iti evamādibhiḥ dānaiḥ sukham yānti yama ālayam sarveṣām eva dānānām nadānām param smṛtam raktam māṃsam vasā śukram kramāt annāt pravardhante śukra adru anti bhūtāni tasmāt anna mayam jagat gandraiḥ ānrī ṣaṅka candana ādibhiḥ samastaiḥ api saṃprāptaiḥ ramanti bahu śritāḥ garbha sthāḥ jāyamānāḥ ca bāla vṛddhāḥ ca madhyamāḥ āhāram bhikāṃśanti deva dānava rākṣasāḥ kṣudhā niḥśeṣa rogāṇām vyādhiḥ śreṣṭhatamaḥ smṛtaḥ sa ca anna oṣadhi lepena naśyati iha na saṃśayaḥ na asti kṣudhā samam duḥkham na asti rogaḥ kṣudhā samaḥ na aśnya roga samam saukhyam na asti koṣa samaḥ ripuḥ annadaḥ prāṇadaḥ prokto prāṇadaḥ ca api sarva daḥ yasya anna pāna puṣṭa aṅgaḥ kurute puṇya saṃcayam anna pradātuḥ tasya arddhe kṛta śrāddhe na saṃśayaḥ trailokye yāni ratnāni bhoga aśrī vāhanāni ca dharma artha mokṣāṇām dehaḥ parama sādhanam annena sadṛśam dānam na bhūtam na bhaviṣyati annam ṛjaskaram loke prāṇāḥ hi anne pratiṣṭhitāḥ dātavyam bhikṣave ca annnam brāhmaṇāya mahātmane kuṭuṃbam pīḍayitvā api tṛptim icchatā viddāti nidhi śreṣṭham yaḥ dadāt annam ārthinne brāhmaṇāya ārta rūpāya pāralaukikam ātmanaḥ śrāntam abhyāni vṛtti arthe gṛhastha gṛham āgatam anna daḥ pūjayet vyāsa suśīlaḥ tu vimatsaraḥ na abhiniṃdet digatam na praṇudyāt kathañcan api śvapāke śuni vā na anna dānam praṇaśyati śrāntāya a dṛṣṭa pūrvāya yaḥ dadyāt pārikhin ca sa samṛddhim avāpnuyāt pitṝn devān tathā viprān atithīn ca mahā śune annam pānam ca śūdrāṇām brāhmaṇe ca viśiṣyate na pṛcchet votra cāraṇam svādhyāyam deśam eva ca bhikṣitaḥ brāhmaṇena iha dadyāt annam ca yaḥ pumān saṃyāti paramam svargam yāvat āśruta saṃbhavam annasya ca vṛkṣāḥ ca sarva kāma phala anvitāḥ bhavanti iha yathā viprāḥ harṣa yukta ādiviṣṭape anna dātuḥ mahā divyāḥ tān śṛṇuṣva mahā śune prakāśante teṣām mahātmanām nānā saṃsthāna rūpāṇi nānā kāma anvitāni ca sarva kāma phala aṃśāḥ api vṛkṣāḥ bhavanam saṃsthitāḥ hema vāpyaḥ śubhāḥ kūpāḥ dīrghāḥ kāśā iva sarvaśas ghoṣayanti ca pānāni śubhāni atha sahasraśas bhakṣya bhojya mayāḥ śailāḥ vāsa āsya ābharaṇāni ca kṣīram sravanti vādyasya parvatāḥ prāsādāḥ pāṇḍura ābhāsāḥ śayyāḥ ca kanaka ojvalāḥ ete lokāḥ puṇya kṛtām anna dānām mahā prabhāḥ tasmāt annam viśeṣeṇa dātavyam mānavaiḥ ghruvam annam prajāpatiḥ sākṣāt annam viṣṇuḥ tvam haraḥ tasmāt anna samam dānam na bhūtam na bhaviṣyati kṛtvā api su mahāt pāpam yaḥ paścāt anna dhaḥ bhavet anna pāna aśva go bāstrāya ācchāsanāni ca preta loke praśastāni dānāni etau viśeṣataḥ evam dāna viśeṣeṇa dharmarāja puram naraḥ yasmāt gāti vimānena tasmāt dānam samācaret yaḥ paṭhet pāṭhayet anyān ca sa bṛddhaḥ prajāyate śṛṇuyāt śāvaye chrādde brāhmaṇān yaḥ mahā śune akṣayyam anna dānam ca pitṛṇām tu patiṣṭhitā iti śrī śivasaṃhāpurāṇe pañcamyā sumāsaṃhitāyām mannadānamāhātmyavarṇanam nāma trayodaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ pānīya dānam paramam dānānām uttamam sadā sarveṣām jīvaṃjunānām tarppṇam jīvanam smṛtam prapādanam mataḥ kuryāt suśīta udi nivāritam bhavet iha loke pare vā api satyam satyam na saṃśayaḥ tasmāt api īśa taḍāgam kārayet naraḥ kūpaḥ pravṛtta pānīyaḥ su pravṛttasya nityaśas sarvē tāryante vaṃśam yasya khāte jalāśaye gāvaḥ pibanti viprāḥ ca sāghavaḥ ca narān sadā nidāgha kāle pānīyam yasya tiṣṭhati a vāritam mṛdu gam viṣamam kṛcchram na kadācid vāpyate taḍāgānām ca vakṣyāmi kṛtānām ye guṇāḥ smṛtāḥ triṣu lokeṣu sarvatra pūjitaḥ yaḥ taḍāgavān mitrātim vijitam kīrtim saṃjananam śreṣṭham taḍāgānām niveśanam taḍāgam śṛṇute yena tasya puṇyam catur vidhi ānām bhūtānām taḍāgaḥ parama āśrayaḥ taḍāga ādīni sarvāṇi diśanti devāḥ manuṣyāḥ gandharvaḥ pitaraḥ nāgarākṣ asāḥ sthāvarāṇi ca bhūtāni saṃśrayanti jalāśayam prāvṛṣ taite taḍāge tu salilam yasya tiṣṭhati tu salilam taḍāge yasya tiṣṭhati vasante ca tathā grīṣme salilam yasya tiṣṭhati atirātrasya medhānām phalam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ mune vyāsa atha vṛkṣāṇām ropaṇe ca guṇān śṛṇu proktam jalāśaya phalam jīva śrīṇane atīta an āgatān sarvān pitṛm vaṃśān tu tārayet kāntāre vṛkṣa ropī yaḥ tasmāt ṛkṣān tu ropayet tatra putrāḥ bhavanti ete pādapāḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ param lokam gataḥ saḥ api lokānām ca akṣayam puṣpaiḥ suraga ṇānām sarvān phalaiḥ cāpi tathā pitṝn chāyayā ca ati hinā sarvān pūjayanti mahīruhāḥ kim ca roga rakṣāṃsi deva gandharva manu syavāḥ gaṇāḥ ca eva saṃśrayanti mahīruhām taḍāga kṛta kṣarāpī ca iṣṭa yajñasya yaḥ dvijaḥ satyam sureṣu jāgatam satyam ca paramam padam satyena eva dhṛtā pṛthvī satye sarve pratiṣṭhitam tapaḥ yajñaḥ puṇyam ca deva ṛṣi pitṛ pūjane satyam yajñaḥ tapaḥ dānam mantrāḥ devī sarasvatī pālanam sarvevedānām sarve tīrtha avagāhanam lakṣāṇi kratavoḥ ca iva satyam eva viśiṣya te satyena devāḥ pitaraḥ mānava uraga rākṣasāḥ prīyante satyataḥ sarve lokāḥ ca sa carācarāḥ satyam āhuḥ param dharmam satyam āhuḥ param padam śṛṇu yaḥ satya niratāḥ tapaḥ śubhuśramam apsaraḥ gaṇa saṃviṣṭaiḥ vimānaiḥ parimātṛbhiḥ snātavyam manasā yuktam sthānam tat param smṛtam ātma arthe vā para arthe vā putra arthe vā api mānavāḥ anṛtam ye na bhāṣante te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ vedāḥ yajñāḥ tathā mantrāḥ santi vipreṣu nityaśas vyāsaḥ uvāca sarveṣām ca eva varṇānām brāhmaṇānām tapodhnam pravakṣyāmi tapodhyāyam sarva kāma artha sādhakam su duścaram dvijātīnām tat me nigaditaḥ śṛṇu tapasā prāpyate svargaḥ tapasā prāpyate yaśaḥ jñāna vijñāna saṃpattiḥ saubhāgyam rūpam eva ca nānāvidhāni vastūni tapasā labhate naraḥ na ātta tapasām prāpyaḥ śaṅkaraḥ parameśvaraḥ kiñcid āsthāya puruṣaḥ tapate tapaḥ tat sarvam samprāpnoti param ca mānaḥ surā pāḥ pāradārī ca brahma ghāḥ gurutalpa gaḥ api sarva īśvara sthaṇuḥ vaiṣṇuḥ śaiva sanātanaḥ brahmā hutāśanaḥ śakraḥ ye ca anye tapasā anvitāḥ aṣṭāśītim sahasrāṇi munīnām ūrdhvarerasām tapasā labhyate rājyam sa ca śakra sura īśvaraḥ tapsā eva prakāśete nakṣrāṇi grahāḥ tathā jñānam vijñānam ārogyam rūpavat tvam tathā eva ca tapasā sṛjyate viśvam brahmā viśvam vinā śramam ghatte śeṣa ukhilām mahīm iti uktam te mahā prājña tapaḥ māhātmyam uttamam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe paścamyām umāsaṃhitāyām tapomāhātmyavarṇanam nāma dvādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ yaḥ adhīte ṛcam ekām hi phalam syāt tat sam mune śruteḥ dhyayanāt puṇyam yat āmoti dvijoṃṂamaḥ tad dhyāpanataḥ ca api dviguṇam phalam aśnute jagat yathā nirālokam jāyate śaśi bhāskaram vinā tathā purāṇam jhā adhyeya marma āpune sadā tapyamānam sadā ajñāna agni śraye yaḥ api śāstrataḥ sambodhayet lokam tasmāt pūjyaḥ purāṇa gaḥ sarvāṣām ca eva pātrāṇām madhye śreṣṭhaḥ purāṇa vid patanāt nāyate yasmāt tasmāt pātram udāhṛtam parti aṇḍucchinnam kartavyā purāṇe kadācana purāṇa jña sarva vetā brahmā viṣṇuḥ hareḥ guruḥ ghanam dhānyam hiraṇyam ca vāsāṃsi vividhāni ca deyam purāṇa vijñāya pareṇa ca ca yaḥ dadāti mahā prītyā purāṇa adhyāya sañjanaḥ pātrāya śubha vastrāṇi sa yāti paramām gatim mahīm gām vā syandanān ca gajanān ca śobhanān yaḥ prayacchati pātrāya tasya puṇya phalam śṛṇu aśva yānam sarva kāmān ca pareṇa ca janmani mahīm dadāti yaḥ tasmai kṛtām phala vartīm śubhām sa tārayet vai vaṃśyān daśa pūrvān daśa parān iha śrutvā akhilān kāmān ate divya śarīravān na yajñaiḥ tuṣṭim āyānti devāḥ prokṣaṇakaiḥ api bilībhiḥ puṣpa pūjābhiḥ nathā pustaka vācanaiḥ viṣṇoḥ ṛkasya kasya api śṛṇu tasya api tat phalam rājasūya aśvamedhānām phalam mā āpnoti mānovaḥ sthitvā rājā bhavati bhū tale bhuṅkte niṣkaṇṭakam bhogān na atra kāyāḥ vicāraṇā itihāsa purāṇābhyām śambhoḥ āyatane śubhe na anyat prīti karam śambhoḥ tat tha anyeṣām divaukasām tathā asya śravaṇam premṇā sarva kāma phala pradam purāṇa śravaṇāt śabhmaḥ niṣpāpaḥ jāyate naraḥ śuklā mogān su vipulān śiva lokam avāpnuyāt rājasūyena yat puṇyam abhiṣṭomrśatena ca tat puṇyam labhate śambhoḥ kathā śravaṇa mātrathaḥ sarva atītha anvagāhena gavām koṭi pradānataḥ ye śṛṇvanti kathāḥ śambhoḥ sadā te manuṣyāḥ na mantavyāḥ rudrāḥ eva na saṃśayaḥ śṛṇvatām śivasakīrtīm santām kīrtayatām ca tām tīrthāni munayaḥ viduḥ gantum niḥśreyasam sthānam ye abhivāñchanti dehinaḥ kathāḥ paurāṇikīm śaivīm bhaktyā śṛṇvantu te sadā kathāḥ paurāṇikīm śrotum yadhi aśaktaḥ sadā bhavet niyata ātmā pratidinam śṛṇuyāt dā muhūrtakam puṇya māsa ādiṣu mune śṛṇuyāt śāṅkarīm kathām śaivīm kathām hi śṛṇvānaḥ puruṣaḥ hi muni īśvara sa nistarati saṃsāram dagdhvā karma mahā aṭavīm kathā śaivīm śṛṇutai vā vā kṣaṇam ca vā ye śṛṇvanti narāḥ bhaktyā na teṣām durgatiḥ bhavet yat puṇyam sarva dāneṣu sarva yajñeṣu vā śune śambhoḥ purāṇa śravaṇāt tapham niścalam bhavet viśeṣataḥ kalau jñāsyeḥ purāṇa śravaṇāt hete paraḥ dharmaḥ na puṃsām hi śuci khyāna paraḥ smṛtaḥ purāṇa śravaṇam śambho nāma saṃkīrtanam tathā kalpadruma phalam ramye manuṣyāṇām na saṃśayaḥ kalau puṃsām hitāya viddhe śambhuḥ purāṇa ākhyam sudhā rasam tibatreṇa ām ute pumān śambhoḥ kathā amṛta pānāt kuśalam eva ajrāmāram yā gatiḥ puṇya śīlānām yajvinām ca tapasvīnām sā gatiḥ sadhasā tāta purāṇa śravaṇāt khal jñāna vāsi tena idā naṣṭā ayoga śāstrāṇi yatnatāḥ adhyetavyāni paurāṇam śāstram śrotavyam eva ca pāpam saṃśīyate nityam dharmaḥ eva vivarddhate purāṇa śravaṇāt jñānī na saṃsāram prapadyate atas eva purāṇāni śrotavyāni prayatnatāḥ dharma artha kāma latbhāya mokṣa mārga āttaye tathā tat phalam samavāpnoti purāṇa śravaṇāt taraḥ na bhaveyuḥ purāṇāni dharma mārga īkṣaṇāni tu yatra sthātā ca atra pātrakam kathāyām ṣaḍīṃśati purāṇānām madhyeṣṭi ekam śṛṇoti yaḥ anyaḥ na dṛṣṭa sukha deaḥ hi purāṇa mārgām hi sadā variṣṭhaḥ śāstram vinā sarvva idam na bhāti sūryeṇa hīnāḥ iva jīva lokāḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe paścamyām umāsaṃhitāyām purāṇamāhātmyavarṇanam nāma trayodaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śastāni cora dānāni mahā dānāni nityaśas pātrebhyaḥ tu pradeyāni ātmānam tārayanti ca hiraṇya dānam go dānam bhūmi dānam dvijottama suvarṇa dānam go dānam pṛthivī dānam eva ca etāni śreṣṭha dānāni kṛtvā pāpaiḥ pramucyate tulādānāni śastāni gāvaḥ pṛthvī sarasvatī nityam gāvaḥ chatram deyāni yācamānebhyaḥ pānam abram tathā eva ca saṃkalpa vihitaḥ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ pradīyate kanakam ca tilāḥ nāgāḥ kanyā dāsī gṛham rathaḥ maṇayaḥ kapalāḥ gāvaḥ mahā dānāni vai daśa gṛhītvā etāni sarvāṇi brāhmaṇaḥ jñāna vid sadā vada anyān tārayet sadyas dhyā ātmānam ca na saṃśayaḥ agnibhiḥ devatāḥ sarvāḥ suvarṇam ca hutāśanaḥ tasmāt suvarṇam da tvā ca dattāḥ syuḥ sarva devāḥ pṛthvī dānam mahā śreṣṭham sarva kāma phala pradum sauvarṇam ca viśeṣeṇa yat kṛtam pṛthunā purā dīyamānām prapaśyanti pṛthvīm rukma asamanvitām atha anyat ca pravakṣyāmi dānam sarva uttamam śṛṇe kāntāram yat na paśyanti yam asyāḥ bahu duḥkha dm kuryāt kāntāra dānam hi vidhinā śuddha mānasaḥ nyāya arjitena dravyeṇa vitta śāṭhya vivarjitaḥ tila prastha mayīm kṛtvā gheṭum sarva guṇa anvitām gheṭu vatsam suvarṇam ca su divyam sarva lakṣaṇam padma ṣaṣ dalam kṛtvā kuṅkuma aktaiḥ śubhaiḥ evam saṃpūjya tām dadyāt brāhmaṇāya sva śaktikaḥ sa ratnam sa hiraṇyām ca sa vibhūṣaṇa bhūṣitām tatas nakam samaśrīyāt dīpān dadyāt vistārāt kārtikyām iti kartavyam pūrṇimāyām prayatnataḥ kṛtvā pāpāni aśeṣāṇi sarvaṃguḥ sa tuḥkha jannaḥ divi saṃkrīḍate vyāsa yāvat indra aśvatardeśe na tena sadṛśam vyāsa param dānam prakīrtitam prayacchate yaḥ kapalām sa vatsām svarṇa śṛṅgikām kāṃsya pātrām rūpya kṣurām sarva lakṣaṇa lakṣitām taiḥ taiḥ guṇaiḥ kāmadudhām bhūtvā sā tulāpuruṣa dānam hi dānānām tulā saṃrohaṇam kārye yadi icchet śreyaātmanaḥ yat kṛtvā mucyate pāpaiḥ ṣaṣ bandhaka tā udbhavaiḥ tulādānam mahat puṇyam sarva pāpa kṣayaṃkaram kṛtvā pāpāni aśeṣāṇi tulādānam karoti yaḥ sarvaiḥ tu pātakaiḥ muktaḥ sa divam yāti asaṃśayam apāpam kṛtam yat ivaseniśāyām dvis saṃkhyayoḥ madhya dine niśā ante vālena vṛddhena mayā hi yuvā jñāna pareṇa pāpam tat sarva evam āśu kṛtam madīyam tulā pumān vai haratu smrāra ariḥ pātre prayuktam draviṇam mayā adya pramāṇapūrṇī nihitam tulāyām tena nā eva sa argham tu mama avaśeṣam kṛta akṛtam yat sukṛtam sametu ca artham tam dadyāt dvijebhyaḥ sarvadā hitaḥ hatvā pāpam divam tiṣṭhyāt vat indra aśvatar deśe iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe pañcamyām umāsaṃhitāyām sāmānyadānavarṇanam nāma caturdaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca dānānām tat mama ākhyāhi mānuṣāṇām hita arthinaḥ śṛṇu kāle pradattasya phalam vindanti mānavāḥ sarva eṣām dānānām tat dadāmi te dānānām dānam brahmāṇḍam khalu mānavaiḥ dātavyam śakti kāmaiḥ tu saṃsāra uttāraṇāya vai tad eka bhāvāt āmi iti sarveṣṭā iva manaḥ rugheṣu kakubhiḥ brahmāṇḍaḥ krīḍate paścāt yāti padam su dulebhataram devaiḥ dhṛte māghavam vyāsaḥ uvāca bhagavan brūhi brahmāṇḍam yat pramāṇam yad ātmakam yad ācāram yathābhūtam yena me pratyayaḥ bhavet mune śṛṇu pravakṣyāmi yat uktam tu brahmāṇḍam tat saṃkṣepāt śrutvā pāpāt pramucyate yat tatāraṇam avyaktam vyaktam tasmāt sa jāyate brahmā dvidhā bhūtāt his kālataḥ brahmāṇḍam sṛjati brahmā caturdaśa bhava ātmakam tasya ādhāraḥ sthitaḥ nāgaḥ ca viṣṇuḥ prakīrtitaḥ śeṣasya guṇān vaktum na śakyāḥ deva dānavāḥ paṭhyate siddaiḥ vārṣa gaṇa pūjitaḥ śiraḥ sāhasra śrutakasya sarvam vidhyotayan diśaḥ phaṇāmaṇi sahasreṇa svasti kāmala dṛṣaṇaḥ mada āghūrṇita netraḥ asau sāmbhiśete ṣṭhavālaḥ śaṃgī kirīṭī bhrāmati yaḥ sa devaiḥ kakuṇḍalaḥ sāyam gaṅgā pravāheṇa nīla vāsāḥ mada udviktaḥ kailāsādiriḥ vā paraḥ yaḥ arcyante nāga kanyābhiḥ svargaṇa vaṇā ambharāt saṃkarṣaṇa ātmakaḥ rudraḥ viṣāna śikhalaḥ ubha jvalaḥ dagdhvā jagatrayam śāntāḥ bhavanti eva anuśuśruma āste śeṣaḥ kṣiti maṇḍalam bibhra sva pṛṣṭhe bhūteśa śeṣa oṃ śeṣa guṇa ācitaḥ tasya vīrya prabāvasya sākāśān śidhraiḥśaiḥ api na hi varṇayitum śakyaḥ svarūpam jñātum eva vā āste kusuma malā iva phaṇāmaṇi śilā aruṇā yadā vijaṃbhate anantaḥ mada āghūrṇita locanāḥ tadā calati bhūḥ eṣā sa āvṛta uya adhika ānanā daśa sāhasramakam pātālam muni sattamam talam talātalam ca āśryam pātālam saptamam matam lokāḥ ime jñeyāḥ vivakṣaṇaiḥ ucchāyaḥ dviguṇa śreṣām sarveṣām ratnam abhayaḥ ratnavantaḥ atha prāsādāḥ bhūmayaḥ hema saṃbhavāḥ teṣu dānava daityāḥ nāgānām jātayaḥ tathā nivasanti mahā nāgāḥ rākṣasāḥ daitya saṃbhavāḥ prāha svargasadaḥ maghye pātālāni iti nāradaḥ nānā bhūṣaṇa bhūṣāḥ tu maṇayaḥ yatra su prabhaḥ āhlādakāni śubhāṇi pātālam kena tat sam pātāle kasya na prītiḥ itas ca itas ca śobhitamam na śītam ātapaḥ yatra kevalam puṃskokila rutam yatra padmāni kamala ākarāḥ na dyaḥ sarāṃsi ramyāṇi dhanyonya vicarāṇi ca bhūṣaṇāni ati śubhāṇi gaṃdha ārbyam ca anulepanam vīṇā veṇu mṛdaṅgānām svanāḥ geyāni ca dvija iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe pañcamyām umāsaṃhitāyām brahmāṇḍakathanepātālalokavaṇane nāma pañcadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ teṣām narkān tān śṛṇuṣva ca mattaḥ śuni vara śreṣṭha pacyante yatra pāpinaḥ vaitaraṇī pūya vahā krimi bhojanasaḥ asīpatravanam ghoram lālābhakṣaḥ ca dāruṇaḥ tathā pūya vahāḥ prāyas bhinet jvālaḥ dhaghāśśirāḥ saṃdaṃśaḥ kālasūtraḥ ca tamaśśāvī cirogdhanaḥ ruṣṭasya mahāraurava śālmalī ityādyāḥ bahavaḥ tatra narkāḥ duḥkha dāyakāḥ pacyante teṣu puruṣāḥ pāpa karmāṇaḥ tu ye kramāt drakṣye tu tān vyāsa sāvadhāna tayā śṛṇu kūṭasākṣyam tu yaḥ vakti vinā viṣṇo surān ca gāḥ śruṇahā svaṇaha tām ca gorodhī viṣa ghātakaḥ tatas kuṃbe durhituḥ tatthā sāṅkhyāḥ vikraya kṛt ca vāc dhekī keśa vikriyī avamantā guruṇām yaḥ paścāt droktā nara aghmaḥ agamya gāmī yaḥ ca ati yāti sapta balam dvija ratna dūṣayitā ca yaḥ sa yāti krimi bhakṣam vai krimīn āti duriṣṭha kṛt pitṛ deva gurūn yaḥ tu nara aghmaḥ lālābhakṣam sa yāti ajñaḥ yaḥ śaṭha kūṭa kuñjaraḥ yaḥ ca antyaja inam saṃsecyaḥ tu yaḥ dvijaḥ a yājya yājakaḥ ca eva tathā iva a makṣya bhakṣakaḥ madhuhastrā mahā āyāti krūrām vaitaraṇīm nadīm te kṛtyam yānti aśaucāḥ ca kulaka ājīvinaḥ ca ye asīpatravanam yāti vṛkṣa chedī vṛthā iva yaḥ vratasya lopakāḥ ye ca sva āśramāt hyutāḥ ca ye saṃdaṃśya atana mādhye patanti bhṛśa a dāruṇe vīryam svameṣṭhu narāḥ brahmacāriṇaḥ putrāḥ na adhyāpitāḥ yaiḥ ca te patanti śvabhojane ete ca anye ca narkāḥ sahasraśas yeṣu duṣkṛta karmāṇaḥ pacyante yātanā gatāḥ tathā eva pāpāni etāni tathā anyāni sahasraśas varṇa āśrami vibhraṃśam ca karma kurvanti ye narāḥ agha viśrori bhedaiḥ ca ye nārakāḥ divi devatāḥ devān aghaḥ bhuktvā sarva anaghān paśyanti nārakāḥ sthāvarāḥ kṛmi pākāḥ ca pakṣiṇaḥ paśavaḥ mṛgāḥ dhārmika ākhi daśāḥ tad hat mokṣiṇaḥ ca yathākramam pāpa kṛt yāti narakam prāyaścitta parāṅmukhaḥ prāyaścittāni kālena manu svāyambhuvaḥ bravīt yāni teṣām aśeṣāṇām karmāṇi uktāni teṣu vai prāyaścittam aśeṣeṇa hara anusmaraṇam param prāyaścittam tu yasya evam pāpam puṃsaḥ prajāyate kṛte pāpeṣu uta apaḥ pi śiva saṃsmaraṇam param māheśvaram avāpnoti madhyāhna ādiṣu saṃsmaran ca saṃdhyāyām kṣīṇa pāpaḥ bhavet naraḥ muktim prayāti svargam vā samasta klśa saṃkṣayam śivasya smaraṇāt eva tasya śambhoḥ amāpateḥ aharniśam śivam tasmāt kṣīṇa aśeṣa pātakaḥ tat eva prītaye bhūtvā punar duḥkhāya jāyate tasmāt duḥkha ātmakam nā asti na ca kiñcid sukha ātmakam manasaḥ pariṇāma uśyam sukha duḥkha upala koṣaṇam jñānam eva param brahma jñānam tattāya kalpate jñāna ātmakam idam idam viśvam sakalam sacarācaram parivijñānataḥ kiñcid bhūyate na param mune evam etat mayā ākhyātam sarve naraka māṇḍalam atas ūrdhvam pravakṣyāmi sāṃpratam maṃḍalam bhuvaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe paṃcamyām umāsaṃhitāyām brahmāṇḍa varṇane narokoddhāravarṇane nāma ṣoḍaśaḥ uśyāyaḥ pārāśarye su saṃkṣepāt śṛṇu tvam vadataḥ mama jabuḥ plakṣa śālmaliḥ ca kuśāḥ krauñcaḥ ca śākakaḥ lavaṇa ikṣu rasaḥ sarpiḥ vai dighudugha jaḥ jalāśāyāḥ jaṃbudvīpaḥ samastarānām etṣām madhyatas sthitaḥ praviṣṭaḥ ṣoḍaśa aghastāt yojanaiḥ tasya ca ucchrayaḥ caturaśīti māna etastaidrīṃtriśat mūrdhni mūle ṣoḍaśa sāhasraḥ karṇikā ākāra saṃsthitaḥ himavān hemakūṭaḥ ca niṣapaghasya dakṣiṇe nīlaḥ śvetaḥ ca śṛṅgī ca uttare varṣaparvataḥ daśasāhasrikāḥ hete ratnavantaḥ aruṇaprabhāḥ sahasra yojana utsedhāḥ tāvat vistarāḥ aiṇaḥ ca te bhāratam prathamam varṣe tatas kiṃpuruṣam smṛtam ramyakam ca uttare pārśve tasya aṃśe tu hiraṇmayam uttare kuravāḥ ca eva yathā vai bhāratam tathā nava sāhasram ekam ekam etāṣām muni sattama ilāvṛtam ṛṣi śreṣṭha catvāraḥ ca atra parvatāḥ viṣkambhāḥ racitāḥ meroḥ ye ojitāḥ punar uñchitāḥ pūrve hi mandaraḥ nāma dakṣiṇe gandhamādanaḥ vipulaḥ paścime bhāge supārśvaḥ ca uttare sthitaḥ kadaṃbaḥ jambū vṛkṣaḥ ca pippalū vaṭaḥ eva ca ekādaśa śata āyāmāḥ pādapāḥ giri ketavaḥ jambūdvīpasya nāmnaḥ vai hetum śṛṇu mahā mune virājate mahā vṛkṣāḥ tad svabhāvam vadāmi te mahāgaja pramāṇāni jambūḥ tasyāḥ phalāni ca patanti bhūbhṛtaḥ pṛṣṭhe śīghrī emāṇāni sarvatas rasena teṣām vikhyātā tatra jambūnadī iti vai tasyāḥ tāṭe sthitānām tud janānām tatra jāyate tīra mṛtsnām ca samprāpya sukha vāyu viśoṣitām jāmbūnada ākhyam bhavati suvarṇam siddha bhuṣaṇam bhadraśvam pūrvatas meroḥ ketumālam ca paścime varṣe dve tu muni śreṣṭha tayoḥ madhye ilāvṛtam vanam caitratham pūrve dakṣiṇe gandhamādanaḥ aruṇodam mahābhadram śīnodam mānam smṛtam sarāṃsi etāni catvāri deva bhōgyāni sarvaśas śītāṃśanaḥ kuruṅgaḥ ca kurraḥ mālyavān tathā ca eke ka pramukhāḥ meroḥ pūrvatas kesara acalāḥ trikūṭaḥ śiśiraḥ ca eva pataṅgaḥ rucakaḥ tathā niṣadhaḥ kapilācāḥ ca dakṣiṇe kesara acalāḥ sinīvāsaḥ kuṭumbaḥ ca kapilū nāradaḥ tathā nāga ādyaḥ ca girayaḥ paścime kesara acalāḥ śaṅkhacūḍa uḍyaḥ ṛṣabhaḥ haṃsaḥ nāma mahīdharaḥ kālam jarā ādyaḥ ca tathā uttare kesara acalāḥ meroḥ upari madhye hi śātakoṭim vidhaiḥ puram caturdaśa sahasrāṇi yojanāni ca saṃkhyayā aṣṭānām lokapālānām paritas tām anukramāt yathādiśam yathārūpam puroṣṭhau upakalpitāḥ tasyām ca brahmaṇaḥ puryām pātayitvā indu maṇḍalam gaṅgā patati vai nadī sītā ca alakananā ca cakṣubhedrā ca vai kramāt sītā pūrveṇa śailam hi nandā ca eva tu dakṣiṇe girīn sakalān catur dikṣu mahā ambudhinam sā yayau prayatā bhūtā gaṅgā tripathagāminī teṣām madhya gataḥ meruḥ karṇikā ākāra saṃsthitaḥ bhārataḥ ketumālaḥ ca bhadrāśvaḥ kuravaḥ tatthā pañcāṇi loka pañcasya mayāt āloka parvatāḥ jaṭharam devakūṭasya āyāme dakṣiṇa uttare gaṃgha mādana keḷāsau pūrva pūcimataḥ gatau jaṭhara ādyāḥ sthitāḥ meroḥ yeṣām dvaḥ dvaḥ vyavasthitau kesarāḥ parvatāḥ uta e śveta ādyāḥ su manāḥ ūrmāḥ śailānām uttare droṇyaḥ siddha ācāraṇa sevitāḥ su ramyāṇi tathā tāṣu kānnāni purāṇi ca sarveṣām ca eva devānām yakṣa gaṃdharva rakṣasām krīḍite devadaite yāḥ śailapāyeṣu ahinī īśam ghimināḥ mālyāḥ bhūte maumāḥ svargāḥ prakīrtitāḥ yāni kiṃpuruṣa ādīni varṣāṇi aṣṭau mahā śune na teṣu śokaḥ na apacyaḥ na idgaḥ kṣudrī ādikam svasthāḥ prajāḥ nirātaṃkāḥ sarva duḥkha vivajitāḥ daśa dva ādaśa varṣāṇām sahasrāṇi sthira āyuṣaḥ sarva itas na teṣu varṣate devaḥ teṣu sthāneṣu kalpanā sattva eteṣu nadyaḥ ca su jātāḥ svarṇa vāḷkāḥ śataśas sānti kṣudrāḥ ca tāṣu krīḍat śumaḥ janaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe pañcamyām umāsaṃhitāyām brahmaṇḍa kathane jambūdvīpavarṣavarṇanam nāma saptadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vakṣye aham bhāratam varṣam dakṣiṇe svarga apavargayoḥ karma bhūmiḥ aṣā smṛtā budhaiḥ nāgadvīpaḥ tathā saumyaḥ gaṃdharvaḥ tu atha vāruṇaḥ ayam tu navamaḥ t teṣām dvīpa sāgara saṃbhṛtaḥ yojanānām sahasram tu dvīpaḥ ayam dakṣiṇa uttaraḥ pūrve kirātāḥ yasya studeḥ kṣiṇe yavanāḥ sthitāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ madhye śūdrāḥ ca bhūyaśas ijyā yuddha praṇāsevāḥ varttaṃtaḥ vyavasthitāḥ mahendraḥ malaya sadyaḥ mudāmā cakṣeparvatāḥ veda smṛti purāṇa ādyāḥ pāriyātra udbhavā mune sarva pāpa harā jñeyā darśanāt sparśanāt api narmadā murasā ādyāḥ ca sapta anyāḥ ca sahasraśas vindhya udbhavāḥ mahā nadyaḥ sarva pāpa hara aśubhāḥ godāvarī bhīmarathī tatāpī praṣukhī niraṃgāḥ pāpa bhaya apahāḥ sahya pāda udbhavāḥ nadyaḥ kṛṣṇaveṇī ādikāḥ tatthā kṛtamālā tāmraparṇī pramukhāḥ malaya udbhavāḥ triyāmā ca ārṣikulyā ādyāḥ mahendra prabhavaḥ smṛtāḥ ṛṣikulyā kumāryā ādyāḥ śuktimat pāda ssaṃbhavāḥ nānā janapādāḥ teṣu maṇḍaleṣu vasanti vai āsām pibaṃti pānīyam ca catvāri bhārate varṣe yugāni āsan mahā śune kṛta ādīni dānāni ca atra dīyante śuklaiḥ ca yājñikaiḥ yatas hi bhūḥ eṣā jambūdvīpe mahā śune atra api bhāratam śreṣṭhataḥ anyāḥ bhoga rūpa mayaḥ atra janma sahasrāṇām māṇuṣyam puṇya sañcayaiḥ gāyanti devāḥ kila gītakāni bhavanti bhūyas puruṣāḥ surāḥ te avāpya māṇuṣya mayam kadācid dhṛtya śambhoḥ paramātma rūpe phalāni sarvāṇi tu karma jāni yāsyāmi aham tattva nu tām hi tasya āpyanti dhanyāḥ khalu te manuṣyāḥ sura īkṣutāḥ karmaṇi sañniviṣṭhāḥ jabuhīm yeṣām khalu bhārate asti te svargam mokṣa ubhaya lābhavantaḥ jambūdvīpaḥ mayā khyātaḥ kṣāra udadhi parisaṃvṛtaḥ saṃveṣṭya kṣāra samuddhim śata sāhasra saṃmitam varṣa acaleṣu ramyeṣu sthitāḥ satatam prajāḥ vasanti devagaṃdharvām varṣeṣu etteṣu nityaśas na āghayaḥ vyāghayaḥ vā api janānām tatra kutrācid daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi tatra jīvanti mānavāḥ atuttā śikhī ca eva pāpajñī tridivam kṛpā amṛtā śuktā ca eva ca nirnagāḥ kṣudra nacyaḥ tathā śailāḥ tatra śata sahasraśas tāḥ pibantu su samṛdhāḥ nadī janpadā astu na tatra api yuga avasthā yathā sthāneṣu saptasu viparīta tvayena āśyāḥ te śūdrāḥ ca muni sattam hariḥ ca bhagavān brahmā yajñaiḥ maṃtraiḥ ca vaidikaiḥ saṃkṣepeṇa tathā bhuyadṛśā śālmalim tvam niśāmaya sapta varṣāṇi tatra eva teṣām nāmāni śṛṇu jīmūtaḥ rohitaḥ tathā śālmalena tu vṛkṣeṇa dvīpaḥ śālmali sañjñakaḥ dviguṇena samudreṇa satatam saṃvṛtaḥ sthitaḥ varṣābhiḥ yañjakāḥ nadyaḥ tāsām nāmāni me śṛṇu śuklā raktā hiraṇyā ca candrā śubhā vimocānā niṣṛtiḥ saptamī tāsām puṇya toyāḥ suśītalāḥ satrā eva tāni varṣāṇi catu varṇa anutāni ca bhagavantam sadā śambhum yajante vividhaiḥ mañtraiḥ devānām tatra sābhiṣyam atīva su manaḥ raume eṣa dvīpaḥ samudreṇa surodena samāvṛtaḥ dviguṇena kuśadvīpaḥ samantāt āhutaḥ tathā eva deva gandharvaḥ yakṣāḥ kiṃpuruṣa ādayaḥ varṇāḥ tatra eva catvāraḥ nija anuṣṭhāna tparāḥ tathā eva ca kuśadvīpe brāhmaṇam ca janārdinam kuśaśayaḥ hariḥ śaiva dyutimān puṣpavān tathā nāmāni sapta ā nāmāni śṛṇu tattvataḥ ghṛtapāpā śivā ca eva pavitra saṃmitaḥ tathā vidyā daṃbhā mahī ca anyā sarva pāpa harāḥ trimāḥ anyāḥ sahasra śaṃsati śubha apaḥ hema bālukaḥ kuśadvīpe kuśa stambhaḥ ghṛtodena samāvṛtaḥ kauśadvīpaḥ mahābhāga śrūyatām ca aparaḥ mahān dviguṇena samudreṇa dighaṃdena ca āvṛtaḥ varṣāṃcalāḥ mahābhuddhe teṣām nāmāni me śṛṇu kauḥ ca vāmanaḥ ca eva tṛtīyaḥ ca aṃgha kārakaḥ divāvṛtiḥ manaḥ ca eva puṇḍarīkaḥ ca dundubhiḥ nivasanti nirāntakāḥ varṣa śaileṣu teṣu vai sarveṣām varṇam eṣu prajāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ ca anukama uditāḥ śāntiḥ ca puṇḍarīkā ca yāḥ pibaṃti payaḥ śubham dīghamaṇḍa udakaḥ ca api śākadvīpena saṃvṛtaḥ dviguṇena adrayaḥ sapta teṣām nāmāni me śṛṇu jhavikescaḥ ca keśarī śākaḥ tatra mahā vṛkṣaḥ tatra puṇyāḥ janapadāḥ cāturvairṇyam samanvitāḥ nāmaḥ ca atra mahā puṇyāḥ sarva pāpa bhaya apahāḥ sukumārī kumārī ca nalinī veṇukā tathā ikṣuḥ ca reṇukā ca eva gabhasti saptamī tathā anyāḥ sahasraśas tatra kṣudra nādyaḥ mahā śune mahī gharāḥ tathā santi śataśas utha sahasraśas dharma dhānine teṣu ira svargāt āgatya mānavāḥ varṣeṣu teṣu pṛthivīm viharanti parasparam śākadvīpe tu vai sūryaḥ prītyā kṣīrodena āvṛtaḥ saḥ api dviguṇena samaṃtataḥ sa vṛtaḥ vyāsa puṣkara āhvayena saṃvṛtaḥ dviguṇena mahā varṣa tatra khyātaḥ atra mānasaḥ yojanānām sahasrāṇi pañca eva u dhvaṃsaṃbhid śṛtaḥ tāni ca eva tu lakṣāṇi sarvatovalī ākṛtiḥ tena eva valī ākārā dvīpa varṣa sama ākṛtiḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi tatra jīvanti mānavāḥ nirāmayāḥ vīta śokāḥ rāga dveṣa vivarjitāḥ mataḥ teṣām na śune satya anṛte na tasya āstām sadā eva vasitaḥ sadā varṣaḥ ca ayam tu kāleja bhoma svarga upama upamaḥ puṣkare ghātakīkhaṇḍe mahāvīte mahā śune nyagrodham puṣkaradvīpe brahmaṇaḥ sthānam uttamam ṛ tasmin nivasate brahmā pūjyamānaḥ sura asuraiḥ svādu dakena nibhinā puṣkaraḥ paribheṣitaḥ evam dvīpāḥ samudreḥ tu sapta saptabhiḥ āvṛtāḥ dvīpāḥ ca eva sakhudāḥ ca samānāḥ dviguṇaiḥ paraiḥ ukta atirikta tā teṣām sa khudreṣu samāni vai jāyante sthālī sthi aṃgi saṃyogāt ghaḥ naḥ muni sattamāḥ atas nyūna atirikta tāḥ ca pakṣayoḥ śukra kṛṣṇayoḥ apām vṛddhi kṣayau dṛṣṭau śataśas tu daśa uttaram sakhudāṇām muni sreṣṭha sarveṣām kathitam tava dviguṇā hiraṇmayī bhūmiḥ sarvaiḥ iṃtu vijitā lokālokaḥ tatas śaila sa sahasrāṇi acalaḥ hi saḥ hi tāvanti yojana ayuta vistṛtaḥ tamaḥ chāṇḍa kaṭāhena sā iyam ūrdhvī mahā śune pañcāśat koṭi vistārā sa dvīpā sa mahī gharā āghāra ghṛtā sarveṣām sarveṣu guṇa adhikā sā iyam kāleya sarveṣām jagatām ilam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe paścamyām umāsaṃhitāyām brahmaṇḍa kathane sapadvīpavaṛṇanam nāma aṣṭādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sānatkumāraḥ uvāca ravi candramasoḥ yāvān mayūkhāḥ hi tāvat sramāṇā pṛthivī mūla ukaraḥ tu gīyate sūmeḥ yojana laḥse tu saṃsthitam ravi maṇḍalam yojanānām sahasrāṇi sadā eva pariḥ a saṃkhyayā śaśinaḥ tu pramāṇāya jagataḥ paricakṣate śaśī tad sthaḥ lakṣa yojana saṃkhyayā mahāṇām maṇḍalam śaśoḥ upari saṃsthitam sa nakṣatram sahasrāṇi daśa eva paritopīḥ bṛhaspatiḥ tat r ūrdhvam tu tasya upāri śanaiścaraḥ saptarṣi maṇḍalam tasmāt cakaṃśeṇa ekena saṃsthitam ṛṣibhyaḥ tu sahasrāṇām śatāt ūrdhve dhruvaḥ sthitaḥ dhruvāt ūrdhvam mahar loka sanma ete brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ sanakāḥ ca sanandāḥ ca tṛtīyaḥ ca sanātanaḥ kapilāḥ ca āsuraiḥ ca eva voḍuḥ pañcaśikhaḥ tathā dvi lakṣa yojanam tasmāt aghaḥ somasutaḥ smṛtaḥ dvi lakṣa yojanam tasmāt ūrdhvam jīvaḥ sthitaḥ guruḥ dvi lakṣa yojanam jīvāt ūrdhvam sauriḥ iti eva sthitaḥ ete sapta ragrahāḥ proktāḥ svara svara āśiṃcaya vasthitāḥ rudra lakṣeṣu yojanataḥ san moghrūm ṛṣayaḥ sthitāḥ vairājāḥ yatra devāḥ vai sthitāḥ dāhi vivarjitāḥ satya dharma tā śā eva jñāninaḥ brahmacāriṇaḥ bhū lokāt hi mānavāḥ tu saṃsiddhāḥ munayaḥ deva rūpiṇaḥ viśvedevāḥ tathā rudrāḥ sādhyāḥ nāgāḥ khaga ādyaḥ nava grahāḥ tatas tatra ṛṣayaḥ vīta kalmaṣāḥ pātālāni ca sā eva brahmāṇḍasya ca vistaraḥ dviṣu kṣa phalam yat dṛti śroṅghvam ghaḥ tathā etat aṇḍa kaṭāhena sarvantaḥ vai samāvṛtam vahninā vāyunā ca api nabhasā tamasā tathā bhūtādinā api mahatā mahāntam ca samāvṛtya pradhānam puruṣaḥ sthitaḥ tena anantam iti khyātaḥ pramāṇam na asti vai yatas aṇḍānām tu sahasrāṇām sahasrāḥ nyutāni ca īdṛśānām prabhūtāni tasmāt avyakta janmanaḥ tathā asau paramātmā vai sarvam vyāpti ātma vedanaḥ ādi vījāt prasuvate tatas tebhyaḥ para iṇḍajāḥ tebhyaḥ putrāḥ tha anyeṣām vījāni anyāni vai tatas mahṛd ādyaḥ viśe pāntāḥ sura ādayaḥ vījādṛkṣa praroheṇa yathā na apacayaḥ taroḥ sūryakānta maṇeḥ sūryāt bṛddhiḥ prajāyate tadvat sa ñjāyate sṛṣṭiḥ śivaḥ tatra na kāmayat śiva śaktiḥ samāyoge deva ādyāḥ prabhavanti hi brahmā viṣṇuḥ ca rudraḥ ca sa śivaḥ parigīyate katā kriyāṇām sarvāsām sa śivaḥ parigīyate vyāsaḥ uvāca santi lokāḥ hi brahmāṇḍāt upari dhānam vā mune santi lokāḥ muni īśvara tān śṛṇu tvam viśeṣeṇa vācyam samāgataḥ virājate mahā dīrghā yatra viṣṇuḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ tasya upariṣṭāt kaumāraḥ lokaḥ hi parama adbhutaḥ senānīḥ ṣaṇmukha tanayaḥ rājate yatra su prabhaḥ yatra śaktiḥ vidhātrikā tri deva jannanī śivā nirguṇā ca svayam devī nirviṃkārā śiva ātmikā tasya upariṣṭāt viśveśyaḥ śiva lokaḥ sanātanaḥ avināśī mahā divyaḥ mahā śobhā anvitaḥ sadā virājate param brahma yatra śaṃbhu maheśvaraḥ tri deva janakaḥ svāmī sarveṣām triguṇāt paraḥ tatra santi śiva priyāḥ tad pālaḥ kṛṣṇa nāmā hi rājate śaṅkara ājñayā pratiṣṭhitiḥ śavena iva śatyā svacchanda cāriṇā vyāsa nirādhāraḥ manoharaḥ śivaḥ tu tad adhiṣṭhātā sarva deva śiromaṇiḥ viṣṇu brahma hareḥ ca sevyaḥ paramātmā niraṃjanaḥ iti te kathitā tāta sarva brahāṇḍa saṃsthitiḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe paṃcamyāḥ sumāsaṃhitāyām lokavarṇanam nāma ekonāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca yat ṛtvā na nivartante śiva bhakti yutāḥ narāḥ parāśara suta vyāsa śṛṇu prītyā śubhām gatim vratam hi śuddha bhaktānām tathā śuddham tapasvinām ye śivam su śuddha tapasā anvitāḥ tapasā divi modante pratyakṣam deva gaṇāḥ ṛṣayaḥ munayaḥ ca eva satyam jānīhi mad vacaḥ tat brahmā nityam viṣṇu hariḥ tatathā devāḥ devyā ukhilāḥ durlabham phalam tatas saṃprāpyate īśau taiḥ ha loke na saṃśayaḥ sāttvikam rājasam ca eva tāmasam trividham smṛtam sāttvikam daivatānām hi yatīnām smṛta airatasyām rājasam dānavānām hi manuṣyāṇām tathā eva ca tāmasam rākṣasāṇām hi narāṇām kura karmmaṇām sāttvikam tat hi nirddiṣṭam aśeṣa phala sādhanam nija deham su saṃpīḍya deha śoṣaka duḥssaḥhaiḥ uttamam sāttvikam vidyāt dharmma buddhiḥ ca niścalā snānam pūjā japaḥ homaḥ śuddha śaucam idam sanam dhīra vidyā satyam akroghū dānam kṣānti demomodyā vāpī kūpa taḍāga ādeḥ prāsādasya ca kalpanā kṛcchram cāndrāyaṇam yajña sum tīrthāni āśramāḥ punar dharma sthānāni ca etāni mukha dāni manīṣiṇām saṃkāliti viṣuva yogaḥ na admuke niyujyatām dhyānam trikālikam jyotiḥ unmanībhāva dhāraṇā recakaḥ pūrakaḥ kumbhaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ trīdhā smṛtaḥ nāḍī saṃcāra vijñānam pratyāhāra niroghnam turīyam buddhi raṇima ādi aṣṭa saṃyutam prāvāttamam samādhiṣṭham para jñāna prasādhanam kāṣṭha avasthāḥ mṛtāvasthāḥ iti īritāḥ vā iti kīrtitāḥ nānā upalaṃbhayoḥ ḍhetā svaiḥ pāpa praṇāśanāḥ nārī śayyā tathā pānam tāmbūla makṣaṇam pañca rāja aiśvaryam vibhūtayaḥ hema bhāraḥ tathā tāmram gṛhāḥ ca ratna ghana tvāḥ pāṇḍityam veda śāstrāṇām gīta nṛtya viḍhūṣaṇam śaṃkha vīṇā mṛdaṅgāḥ ca gaja indraḥ chatram ca āmere ca etāni pumān ādṛśam vanuḥ snehaiḥ stala vat sa niṣpīḍyate aram gaccha iti ca api enam kurute jñāna mohitaḥ jānu api iha saṃsāre bhrāmate ghaṭīyantrā vat sarva yoniṣu duḥkha ārtaḥ tathā avareṣu careṣu ca kāla antara vaśāt yāti mānuṣya mati durlabham mānuṣyam prāpyate puṇya gauravāt vicitrāḥ gatayaḥ proktāḥ karmaṇām gurulāghavāt mānuṣyam ca samāsādya svarga mokṣa prasādhanam na ācaret śreyaḥ ca mṛta śocyate ciram deva asurāṇām sarveṣām mānuṣyam ca ati durlabham durlabham prāpya mānuṣyam dhṛthā tat janya kīrtitam dharma mūlam hi mānuṣyam labdhvā sva arthesādhanam yadi lābhāya yatnaḥ syāt mūlam rakṣet svayam tatas na ācaret yā ātmanaḥ śreyaḥ cetanaḥ dvīpānām eva sarveṣām karmaṇā bhariyam ucyate itas svargaḥ ca mokṣaḥ ca prāpyate deśe smin abhārate varṣe prāpya mānuṣyam dhruvam na kuyāt ātmanaḥ śreyaḥ tena ātmā khalu vañcitaḥ yāvat svāsthyam śarīrasya tāvat dharmam samācaret adhruveṇa śarīreṇa dhruvam yaḥ na prasādhayet āyuṣaḥ khaṇḍa khaṇḍāni tad agratāḥ yadā na jñāyate mṛtyuḥ kadā kasya bhaviṣyati na dadāti kadā kasmāt ghanam gṛhīta dāna pātheyaḥ sukham yāti yama ālaym yeṣām kāleya puṇyāni pāripūrṇāni gacchantām svarga deśam hi teṣām lābhaḥ pade pade īm iti jñātvā naraḥ puṇyam kuyāt pāpam vivarjayet ye manāk api deveśam prapaṇna śaraṇam śivam teṣām api ghoram na paśyanti yamam na narakam tathā pāpaiḥ mahā mohaiḥ kiñcid kāle śiva ājñayā na teṣām naraka ādi iti muni sattama para loka asya pāthayyam mokṣa upāyam anāmayam śiva nāma eva sāra mahāroga eka śāmakam nā anyat saṃsāra urasya śāmakam darśyate mayā brahmahatyā sahasrāṇi purā kṛtvā tu pulkaśaḥ śivā iti nāma vimalam śrutvā mokṣam gataḥ purā śiva bhaktyā mahā prājña muktim muktim ca vindati iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe pañcamyām umāsaṃhitāyām matuuviśeṣakathanam nāma viṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca brāhmaṇa tvam hi duṣprāpyam nisargāt brāhmaṇaḥ bhavet īśvarasya mukha lākṣyaḥ vākubhyām ūrtaḥ viśaḥ pādyām śūdraḥ samutpannaḥ iti tasya mukhalat śūtiḥ duṣkṛtena tu kāle sthānāt dṛśyanti mānavāḥ śreṣṭham sthānam samāsādya paṇḍitaḥ brāhmaṇyāt sa paribrāṣṭaḥ kṣatriya tvam niṣevate janma antara sahasrāṇi tamasyaḥ āviśate yatas tasmāt prāpya param sthānam pramādena tu nāśayet sva sthānam sarvadā rakṣet prāpya api vipadraḥ naraḥ brāhmaṇa tvam śubham prāpya brāhmaṇyam yaḥ avasanyate karmaṇā yena medhāvī śūdraḥ vaiśyaḥ hi jāyate śūdraḥ bhūtvā samācaret kurute kāmayān stu śūdraḥ api vaiśya tām vrajet agnihotram upādāya śeṣa anaktabhojanaḥ sa vaiśyaḥ kṣatriya kule jāyate na atra saṃśayaḥ kṣatriyaḥ jāyate yajñaiḥ saṃskṛtaiḥ ācchad dakṣiṇaiḥ adhīte svargam anvicchan ṛgvetāmi śaraṇam sadā ahnu kāla abhigāmī ca svabhāvī ādham anatparaḥ go brāhmaṇa gārmaṇaḥ asti hi saṃgrāma abhihataḥ bhavet brāhmaṇa tvam hi duṣprāpyam kuṇḍreṇa sādhyate naireḥ brāhmaṇyā prāpyam mokṣam ca api muni īśvara vyāsaḥ uvāca etat diś ca ahyam śrotum brūhi tvam vadatām vara agnihoma dimiḥ śāriṣṭhāḥ vipula dakṣiṇaiḥ na tat phalam avāpnoti saṃgrāme yat vāpnuyāt iti prāhuḥ yajña karmāṇi daṃśa dā tasmāt te pravakṣyāmi yat phalam śastra ājīvinām dharma alābhaḥ atha īṃ lābhaḥ ca yaśaḥ lābhaḥ tathā eva ca yaḥ śūraḥ vāñchate yuddham viṣṇu loke sa jāyeta yaḥ ca yuddheṣu parājitaḥ rājā vā rāja putraḥ vā senāpatiḥ atha api vā hataḥ kṣatreṇa yaḥ śūraḥ tasya lokaḥ uda kṣayaḥ bhavet yāvanti tasya romāṇi bhidyante aśvaimeṃhāhve tāvataḥ labhate lokān sarva ekāmaduṣhā skhyān vīrāsanam vīraśayyā vīrasthāna sthitiḥ ca sthirā gavā arthe brāhmaṇa arthe ca sthānaḥ svāmi artheṣu iva ca ye mṛtāḥ te sukham yānti yathā mukti nanaḥ tathā yaḥ kaścid brāhmaṇam hatvā paścāt prāṇān parityajet ātma deha parityāgaḥ su duṣkaraḥ yuddham puṇyatamam svargye rūpa jñam sarvetoṣukṣam sarvām varṇānām kṣatriyasya viśeṣataḥ bṛśam ca eva pravakṣyāmi yuddha dharmam sanātanam yādṛśāya grahaṭavyam yādṛśam parivarjanīyat ātatāyinam māyā antam api vedāntam dvijam haṃtā api asau na haṃtavyaḥ pānīyam yaḥ ca yācate raṇe hatvā āturān vyāsaḥ sa naraḥ brahma ghāḥ bhavet vyāghātam durbaram bālam strī nātham kṛpaṇam dhruvam evam vicārye sat dhīmān bhave aprītyā raṇapriyaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe paścamyāḥ sumāsaṃhitāyām raṇaphalavarṇanam nāma ekaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca tāta vadet idānīm jīva janma vighānataḥ śṛṇu vyāsa samāsena śāstra sāram aśeṣatas vāyunā ghāmyamānaḥ agni rati uṣṇam kurute jalam dvidhā bhavati tat pakam pṛthak kīṭam pṛthak rasaḥ karṇāḥ chinā nasikāḥ jihvā dantāḥ śiśnaḥ gudam nakhāḥ mala āśrayaḥ kaphaḥ svedaḥ viṣ mūtram dvādaśa smṛtāḥ hat padme pratibaddhāḥ ca sarva nāḍyaḥ saṃtatāḥ jñeyāḥ rasma vāhinyaḥ tad makāram śune tāsām mukheṣu tam sūkṣmam prāṇa sthāpayate rasam rasena tena nāḍīḥ tāḥ prāṇam pūryate punar punar prayāti saṃpūrṇaḥ tāḥ ca deham samantataḥ tatas sa nāḍī madhyasthyaḥ śarīrīṇā ātmanā rasaḥ tvac tayā veṣṭyate pūrvaiḥ ruhiram ca prajāyate raktāt śomānim māṃsam ca keśāni snāyuḥ ca māṃsataḥ snāyutaḥ ca tathā asthīni nakhāḥ mañja asthi saṃbhavāḥ mañjā kāraṇa vaikalyam śukram hi prasava ātmakam iti dvādaśā adharmasya pariṇāmaḥ prakīrtitaḥ śukraḥ uśrā jāyate saṃbhavaḥ ṛtu kāle yadā śukram nirdoṣam yoni saṃsthitam tadā tad āyuḥ saṃspṛṣṭam strī raktena ekatam vrajet visaṅga kāle śukrasya jīvaḥ kāraṇa saṃyutaḥ saṃvṛtaḥ prāviśa uddhinī karma abhiḥsvairiṇī ojitaḥ pañca rātreṇa kililam budbuda ākā ārtām vrajet bududaḥ sapta rātreṇa māṃsa peśī bhavet punar śiraḥ ca skandhau ca pṛṣṭhavaṃśaḥ tathā ubdaram pāṇi pādam tathā pārśve kaṭi gātram tathā eva ca tribhiḥ māsaiḥ prajāyante sarvam aṅkura saṅghayaḥ mukham nāsā ca karṇau ca māsaiḥ pañcabhiḥ eva ca danta paṃktiḥ tathā guḍham jāyate ca nakhāḥ punar karṇayoḥ tu bhavet chidram ṣaṣ māsa abhyantareṇa tu ca nābhiḥ śrābhiḥ upajāyate saṃghayaḥ ye ca gātreṣu sabhiḥ aṅga pratyaṅga saṃpūrṇaḥ paripakvasya tiṣṭhati mātuḥ āhāra cauryeṇa ṣaḍguṇena rasena tu tatrasthitim labhet jīvaḥ saṃpūrṇa iṃsimaḥ śarīrake mukham duḥkham vijānāti nidrā svam purā kṛtam mṛtaḥ śainam punar a jātaḥ punar śainam puna mṛtaḥ nānā yoni sahasrāṇi mayā dṛṣṭhāni jāyatām addhunā jāta mātra ūham prāka saṃskāraḥ eva ca śreyaḥ asmunā kariṣyāmi yena garbhe na saṃbhavaḥ anveṣyāmi śiva jñānam saṃsāra vinivartakam evam sam garbheduḥkhena mahatā paripīḍitaḥ jīvaḥ karma śādāḥ te mokṣa upāyam vicintayan yathā giri vara kāntaḥ kaścid duḥkhena tiṣṭhati tathā jarayuṇā dehī duḥkham tiṣṭhati veṣṭitaḥ garbhāvāsāt param duḥkham kaṣṭam nā eva asti kutracid dehinām duḥkha bhūlam su ghoram iti saṃkaṭam nām parikīrtitam kevalam sapta māsaḥ bhavassdā garbhātsdulam duḥsam yoni yantra nipīḍanāt bhavet pāpa ātmanā ikṣu vat pīḍyamānasya yantreṇa eva samantataḥ śirasā tāḍyamānasya ca yantreṇa pīḍita yat agniḥ sāraḥ tsthutisthalā kṣaṇāt tathā śarīram nissāram yoni yantra nipīḍanāt rakta māṃsa mṛdā ālim viṣṇutra dravya bhājanasam mahā dvāram gavākṣa ādaka bhūṣitam oṣṭha dvaya kapāṭa ca tathā jihvā gaṃla anvitam bhoga tṛṣṇā ātura mūḍha rāga dveṣa vaśa anugam jarāyu pariṃveṣṭitam yoni mārgaṇa viṣṇuta rakta sikta aṅgam vikośa ika samudbhavam śatam ṣaṣṭyā adhikam pañca peśīśatā sārdhibhiḥ tisamibhiḥ chanam samantāt romakōṭibhiḥ śarīram hi tāḥ smṛtāḥ etāvatībhiḥ nāḍībhiḥ koṭibhiḥ te dvādaśa daśanāḥ proktāḥ viṃśatiḥ ca nakhāḥ smṛtāḥ pittasya kuḍavam jñeyam kafasya athā kam smṛtam vasāyāḥ ca palam kapilasya ca pañca adhe tu tulā jñeyā palāni daśa medasaḥ pala trayam mahāraktam mañjāyāḥ ca caturguṇam śukra ucche kuḍavam jñeyam tat bījam dehinām balam māṃsasya ca eka pīḍena pala sāhasra śucyate raktam pala śatam jñeyam viṣṇumatram yad pramāṇataḥ aña iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe paśmyāśumāsaṃhitāyām nāma dvāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śṛṇu vyāsa mahābuddhe dehaḥ ti āśu citām śṛṇe mahatvam ca svabhāvasya śukra śoṇita saṃyogāt deha saṃjāyate yatas nityam na ayam aśuci smṛtaḥ yathā antiviṣṭhayā pūrṇaḥ śucimāna bahis ghaṭaḥ śodhyamānaḥ hi dehaḥ ayam tena ayam aśuciḥ tatataḥ saṃgrāpya atipavitrāṇi pañcagavyam harviṣi ca aśuci tvam kim anyat aśuciḥ tatataḥ hṛdyāni api avra pānāni yam prāpya surabhīṇi ca aśuci tvam prayānti āśu kim anyat aśuci s t taḥ he janāḥ kim paśyanti dine dine sva dehāt kaśmalam pūtiḥ tad ādhāraḥ katham śuciḥ dehaḥ saṃśodhyamānaḥ api pañcagavya kuśa ambubhiḥ ghṛṣyamāṇaḥ iva aṅgāraḥ nirmala tvam na gacchati karpūra purīṣa ādyaiḥ tad dehaḥ śudhyate katham sarvām śuci nidhānasya śarīrasya na vidyate śuciḥ ekāḥ pradeśaḥ api viṣṇmasya iva hṛteḥ eva smṛt ātma deśa śrotāṃsi śodhyate karaḥ tathā api dasya na vibhraṃśyanti kiṃkarāḥ kāya sugandha dhūpa ādyaiḥ nena api susaṃskṛtaḥ yathā jātyā eva kṛṣṇaḥ arthaḥ śuktrasya yāntrī upāyataḥ saṃśodhyamānā api tathā bhavet vṛttiḥ nirmalā aho mohasya māhātmyam yena idam chāditam jagat śīghram paśyan svakam doṣam kāyasya na virajyate virāga kāraṇam tasya kim etat upādiśyate gaṅgā toyena sarveṇa mṛd varaiḥ pavita upamaiḥ tīrthesnānaiḥ tapobhiḥ vā duṣṭa ātmā nā eva śudhyati śhṛtitaḥ śāli tā tīrthe kim śudhim āvigacchati ājānmanaḥ jñāna paraḥ manuṣyaḥ na śudhyati iti eva vayam vadāmaḥ prajvālya vahnim ghṛta taila siktam pradakṣiṇa āvartita śvanam mahāntam gaṅgā ādi tīrtheṣu vasanti matsyāḥ devālaye pakṣi gaṇāḥ ca nityam bhāvoijñatāḥ te na phalam labhante tīrtha avagāhāt ca tathā eva dānāt bhāva śuddhiḥ param śaucam pramāṇam sarva karmaṇu kāntā bhāvena duhitā anyathā paśyatva masya bhāvasya mahābhāgyam aśeṣatas pariṣvaktaḥ api bhāva hīnam na kāmayet nādhā ādibhiḥ viṣa mantraiḥ ca bhakṣyāṇi surabhīṇi ca yadi cintā samādhatte citte kāma ādiṣu triṣu bhāvataḥ śuciḥ śuddhaḥ ātmā svargam mokṣam ca vindati bhāvena eka ātma śuddha ātmā dahan ca dhrastruvan smṛtaḥ lokān tu bahu yājinām jñāna malam bhasā puṃsām sadrāgya smṛdā punar tvac mātra sāram nissāram kadlīsāra sannibham jñātvā evam doṣavat deham yaḥ prājñiḥ śithilaḥ bhavet deha bhoga udrvak nāvāt śami cittaḥ prasaṅg dhīḥ saḥ
